     Risks & mitigations

     - Flat-search SIMD performance. Hand-rolled with wide::f32x8 should land
     within 2Г— of FAISS's native SIMD on Apple Silicon. Mitigation: Phase 0.1
     spike measures this directly. If we're slower than 10ms per query at 103k
     chunks, fall back to usearch (single-header, mmap, mature; ~half-day swap).
      Decision point inside Phase 0, day 1.
     - mmap correctness on Linux/macOS/Windows. memmap2 handles all three but
     Windows file-locking semantics differ. Mitigation: deferred until Phase 0.2
      cross-compile CI exercises Windows; if Windows mmap is fragile, gate the
     Windows binary on --no-mmap mode (read-into-Vec) until fixed.
     - GDrive OAuth in Rust. yup-oauth2 requires either service-account JSON
     (cleanest) or an installed-app flow with localhost callback. Mitigation:
     require service-account JSON for v1; document how to create one. The Python
      path used gcloud auth application-default login which is convenient for
     the user but harder to match in Rust without shelling out.
     - Async/sync split in CLI. ragrep "query" doesn't need an async runtime
     (one HTTP call to Voyage rerank). Spinning up tokio for that is overkill
     (~5ms cost). Mitigation: embed:: and rerank:: expose both sync (ureq) and
     async (reqwest) variants; the CLI search path uses sync, the serve
     subcommand uses async.
     - tiktoken vs Voyage tokenizer drift. Voyage uses its own tokenizer; we'd
     be using cl100k_base. For chunk-size enforcement (512 tokens) the drift is
     small (вүӨ5% chunk-count differences in practice). Mitigation: accept the
     drift; chunks aren't required to be exactly 512 tokens. If Voyage rejects
     an oversize batch we already retry.
     - Pickle migration robustness. The migration script must read whatever
     pickle protocol Python wrote. Mitigation: the script runs in the user's
     existing venv (which has the same pickle/Python version that wrote it), so
     this is a non-issue. Document the venv requirement in MIGRATION.md.
     - Scope creep. 10вҖ“12 weeks part-time is a lot. Mitigation: Phase 1 is the
     ship-gate. After Phase 1, users get the latency win immediately. Phases 2вҖ“5
      can take as long as they take without blocking value.

     Notes: Biggest scraper; sets the complexity-budget bar

     Verification recipe (end-to-end)

     After Phase 0.1 (spike) ships:

     # Extract embeddings from existing FAISS index
     python tools/extract_embeddings.py data/index/
     ls -la data/index/embeddings.bin                          # expect 
     423,329,792 bytes

     # Build the spike
     cargo build --release

     # Spike parity check (uses query embeddings extracted from Python)
     python tools/spike_parity.py                               # writes 3 query
      JSON files + Python top-10
     ./target/release/ragrep --query data/spike/q_auth.json     # expect same 
     top-10 indices
     ./target/release/ragrep --query data/spike/q_deploy.json
     ./target/release/ragrep --query data/spike/q_incident.json

     # Bench
     ./target/release/ragrep --query data/spike/q_auth.json --bench 10  # expect
      <10ms p50

     After Phase 1 ships:

     # Build for current platform
     cargo build --release

     # Smoke test
     ./target/release/ragrep --help                            # <20ms expected
     ./target/release/ragrep                                   # shows splash

     # One-time migration: chunks.pkl + embed_cache.pkl вҶ’ msgpack 
     (extract_embeddings already ran in Phase 0.1)
     python tools/migrate.py data/index/

     # Parity test against Python
     ./tools/parity.sh                                         # 50 queries, 
     вүҘ90% top-10 overlap

     # End-to-end search
     ./target/release/ragrep "auth" -m grep -n 5
     ./target/release/ragrep "auth" -m hybrid -n 5
     ./target/release/ragrep "auth" --json | jq

     # Server mode (uses existing Python server)
     RAGREP_SERVER=http://localhost:8321 ./target/release/ragrep "auth"

     # Cross-compile sanity
     cross build --release --target aarch64-apple-darwin
     cross build --release --target x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu

     After Phase 5 ships:

     # From clean Docker
     docker run --rm -it debian:bookworm-slim bash -c \
       "apt-get update && apt-get install -y curl ca-certificates && \
        curl -fsSL https://ragrep.cc/install.sh | sh && \
        ~/.local/bin/ragrep --help && \
        RAGREP_SERVER=https://your-cloud-run.run.app ~/.local/bin/ragrep 'auth'"

     What stays after Phase 5

     - docs/ (landing page, install.sh, fonts) вҖ” unchanged content, install.sh
     now downloads binary
     - tools/migrate.py вҖ” kept indefinitely so old-Python users can still
     migrate
     - config.toml format вҖ” same TOML shape, fully readable by Rust
     - .env / .env.example вҖ” same env vars
     - data/index/ layout вҖ” same files, msgpack instead of pickle for
     chunks/embed_cache
     - GitHub repo URL (github.com/fntune/ragrep) вҖ” same
     - Vanity domain (ragrep.cc) вҖ” same

     What goes:
     - pyproject.toml, src/ragrep/, uv.lock, Makefile (replaced by justfile or
     just cargo commands)
     - requirements.txt Cloud Run target (replaced by Dockerfile building the
     Rust server binary)
     - All Python deps (voyageai already gone, faiss-cpu/rank-bm25/torch/transfo
     rmers/sentence-transformers/google-genai/etc.)

вҸә Spike result: parity вң“, latency 3Г— over target.

  - Correctness: top-7 match exactly across all 3 queries; the only "DIFF" rows
  in the incident query (ranks 8/9) are tied scores in different order вҖ” same
  chunks, same f32 score values to 6 decimals. That's tie-break order, not a
  bug.
  - mmap load: 16вҖ“34Вөs (target was <2ms, we're 50вҖ“100Г— under)
  - Search latency: 29ms warm (target was <10ms вҖ” we're 3Г— over)
  - First-query cold: 619ms while OS page cache fills

  29ms is faster than Python's hybrid path overall, but I want to know if we're
  leaving SIMD on the table. Quick experiment with target-cpu=native:

вҸә Bash(sysctl -n machdep.cpu.brand_string hw.ncpu 2>&1; cd
      /Users/sour4bh/dev/ragrep/rust && RUSTFLAGS="-C target-cpu=native" cargo
      build --release 2>&1 | tail -5 && .вҖҰ)

вҸә рҹҺҜ 7.9ms p50 with RUSTFLAGS="-C target-cpu=native" on the M4 Max вҖ” well under 
  the 10ms target.

  The default release profile was conservative ARM64 (NEON only, no FMA). Native
   target enables the M4's full SIMD pipeline. For shipping we'll fix this with
  a profile target-cpu=apple-a14 baseline (M1 floor, gets ~80% of the gains
  across all Apple Silicon).

  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ numpy @ (Accelerate BLAS)   в”Ӯ 2.27ms в”Ӯ 2.54ms в”Ӯ 2.88ms в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  No вҖ” we're ~35% slower than FAISS (and ~3Г— slower than numpy's BLAS-backed
  matmul, which both of them lose to).

  That's a more honest data point than my earlier ~6ms FAISS estimate. The gap
  exists for one big reason:

  - Our spike is single-threaded. wide::f32x8 is great SIMD but one core is one
  core. Numpy and FAISS both multi-thread the search across cores via
  OpenMP/Accelerate. On a 14-core M4 Max that's a 5вҖ“10Г— headroom we're not
  using.

  Three ways to close (and beat) the gap:

  approach: rayon parallel search across N cores
  expected p50: ~1вҖ“1.5ms
  cost: 1 dep, ~5 LOC change
  tradeoffs: Pure Rust, scales with cores. Probably beats numpy/FAISS.
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  approach: matrixmultiply crate (pure Rust GEMM)
  expected p50: ~3вҖ“4ms
  cost: 1 dep, ~10 LOC
  tradeoffs: Single-threaded but better SIMD scheduling than wide.
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  approach: accelerate-src (link Apple Accelerate)
  expected p50: ~2.5ms
  cost: macOS-only dep
  tradeoffs: Matches numpy speed on macOS, but breaks our "single static binary,

    no system deps" story on Linux.

  My pick: rayon. Pure Rust, no platform-specific deps, scales linearly across
  cores. The index::flat::Flat::search becomes:

  use rayon::prelude::*;
  let scored: Vec<(f32, u32)> = (0..self.n)
      .into_par_iter()
      .map(|i| (inner_product(query, &embs[i*self.dim..(i+1)*self.dim]), i as
  u32))
      .collect();

  Want me to add rayon to the spike and re-bench? I'd expect us to land
  somewhere around 1.5ms вҖ” comfortably faster than both FAISS and numpy on this
  hardware. ~15 minutes of work.

  We're faster than FAISS, faster than numpy/Accelerate, in pure Rust, with one
  tiny dep, mmap-loaded with no copy, and zero C++ build deps.

  One honest caveat: rayon's thread pool inits lazily on first parallel call вҖ”
  that's a one-time ~6ms cost per process. For CLI use (one search per
  invocation) the real-world numbers are ~8ms cold, ~2ms if you do multiple
  searches in the same process (REPL, server, batch). We can fold that 6ms init
  into the splash/index-load phase by pre-warming the pool, which I'd do as part
   of Phase 0.2.

  Where do you want to go from here:

  subcommands, Actions matrix, install.sh)
  2. Polish the spike further вҖ” pre-warm the rayon pool, try matrixmultiply to
  see if it's still even faster, measure cold-start in detail
  3. Something else

вң» Cogitated for 1m 38s

вқҜ > We can fold that 6ms init into the splash/index-load phase by pre-warming   
  the pool                                                                      
  explain                                                                       

вҸә What rayon does today:

  into_par_iter() lazily creates a global thread pool the first time it's
  called. Spawning N OS threads + setting up rayon's work-stealing queues costs
  ~6ms on the M4 Max. That's why the first search shows ~8ms (6ms pool init +
  2ms actual work) and subsequent searches show ~2ms.

  If a CLI user runs ragrep "auth", that's one process, one search вҶ’ they pay
  the full 8ms. The 2ms p50 in the bench is misleading for CLI use because the
  bench loop reuses the same warm pool.

  What "pre-warming" means:

  Trigger the pool init before search starts, so it overlaps with work the user
  is already waiting for. Concretely, somewhere very early in main():

  // In main, before any user-visible work
  rayon::ThreadPoolBuilder::new()
      .num_threads(num_cpus::get())
      .build_global()
      .unwrap();

  Or even simpler вҖ” kick off a no-op parallel iteration:

  rayon::iter::repeatn((), 1).for_each(|_| ());

  Either forces the pool to spin up its threads.

  Why "fold into splash/index-load":

  The CLI's first ~10ms is doing other necessary work anyway:

  1. Parse argv (clap) вҖ” ~50Вөs
  2. Load .env files вҖ” ~200Вөs
  3. Load config.toml вҖ” ~100Вөs
  4. Open and mmap embeddings.bin вҖ” ~30Вөs (we measured)
  5. Open and read chunks.msgpack вҖ” ~5вҖ“10ms (this one's real I/O for 200MB)
  6. Build BM25 index from msgpack вҖ” ~5ms

  Steps 5 and 6 can run on the main thread while rayon is spinning up its
  workers in the background. The OS scheduler puts the rayon workers on idle
  cores; they're ready by the time the search loop starts. Total wall time is 
  unchanged, but the search itself measures 2ms instead of 8ms because the pool
  init was hidden behind I/O.

  Even better: spawn it on a background thread before any blocking work:

  fn main() {
      // Fire-and-forget pool init on a detached thread.
      // By the time we call `flat.search()`, rayon's workers are usually live.
      std::thread::spawn(|| {
          rayon::iter::repeatn((), 1).for_each(|_| ());
      });

      // Now do the normal CLI flow: parse args, load config, mmap, read chunks,
   search.
      // ...
  }

  The spawn itself costs ~50Вөs. The rayon init now runs in parallel with
  everything else main() does. By the time flat.search() calls into rayon, the
  pool is already initialized in 99% of cases.

  What this doesn't help:

  - It doesn't make total wall time shorter вҖ” we still do the same amount of
  work.
  - It doesn't help if there's literally nothing else to do (e.g., ragrep 
  --query <vec> with no chunks-file load, like our spike).
  - It doesn't help on tiny single-core systems where there are no cores to
  spare.

  What it does help:

  - The user-visible "search took Xms" number drops from 8ms to 2ms.
  - For server mode (ragrep serve), the pool inits once at startup and stays
  warm вҖ” every request is the 2ms number, no cold-start cost.

  For the CLI's ragrep "auth" flow with the full Phase 1 pipeline (mmap + chunks
   load + BM25 load + search + rerank HTTP), the chunks/BM25 load takes longer
  than rayon init, so background-spawning the pool init means search latency
  genuinely measures ~2ms in production, not 8ms.

  Tiny optimization, but free. I'd put it in cli::search::run as the very first
  line.

  Branch rust is pushed. The pre-warm rayon task is still pending вҖ” it's a Phase
   1 polish item, not a Phase 0 blocker.

  Phase 0 commits on rust branch:
  - c915b66 вҖ” spike: mmap + brute-force IP search
  - 744dbc5 вҖ” rayon parallel (3.7Г— speedup, beats FAISS)
  - 5a288a3 вҖ” full module tree + clap subcommands + 1.7ms startup
  - a988548 вҖ” CI matrix + binary installer

  Phase 1 is the next big chunk (~2 weeks of work). It splits into clean
  sub-pieces:

  1. Index store + load вҖ” port chunks.pkl migration, hand-roll BM25, wire
  index::store::load to return (Flat, Vec<Chunk>, BM25). Unblocks everything
  search-related.
  2. HTTP embedders + reranker вҖ” port VoyageEmbedder.embed_query and
  VoyageReranker.rerank to reqwest. ~2 days.
  3. query::{grep, semantic, hybrid} вҖ” public engine API. Calls into retrieve +
  rerank.
  4. cli::search::run вҖ” wire it all together; clap args вҶ’ engine. Make ragrep 
  "auth" end-to-end work.
  5. cli::search::proxy вҖ” server mode (Cloud Run identity tokens etc.).

  Where to start? My instinct is (1) вҶ’ (3) вҶ’ (4) without (2) вҖ” that gets ragrep 
  "auth" -m grep and ragrep "auth" -m semantic working end-to-end against a
  Python-built index migrated to msgpack, deferring rerank (and therefore full
  hybrid mode) until last. Each sub-step is shippable on its own; we can release
   v0.1.0-rust after step 4 and let users try it.

  Want me to proceed with that order, or do you want a different sequencing?

      80              v = v.astype("float32").tolist()
      81          else:
      82              v = list(map(float, v))
      83 -        if not isinstance(k, (bytes, bytearray)):

      85 +        elif not isinstance(k, (bytes, bytearray)):            
      86              k = bytes(k)
      87          serializable.append([k, v])

вҸә Write(rust/src/index/bm25.rs)
  вҺҝ В Added 138 lines
        1 +//! Okapi BM25 over whitespace+lowercase tokens.              
        2 +//!                                                           
        3 +//! Mirrors `rank_bm25.BM25Okapi` (which `src/ragrep/ingest/st
          +ore.py` uses):                                                
        4 +//! same k1=1.5, b=0.75, IDF formula `ln((N - df + 0.5) / (df 
          ++ 0.5) + 1)`.                                                 
        5  
        6 +use std::collections::HashMap;                                
        7 +                                                              
        8 +use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};                          
        9 +                                                              
       10 +const K1: f32 = 1.5;                                          
       11 +const B: f32 = 0.75;                                          
       12 +                                                              
       13 +#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]               
       14 +pub struct Bm25 {                                             
       15 +    /// Doc length (token count) per document.                
       16 +    doc_lens: Vec<u32>,                                       
       17 +    /// Average doc length.                                   
       18 +    avg_doc_len: f32,                                         
       19 +    /// term -> Vec<(doc_idx, term_freq_in_doc)>              
       20 +    postings: HashMap<String, Vec<(u32, u32)>>,               
       21 +    /// term -> idf                                           
       22 +    idf: HashMap<String, f32>,                                
       23 +    /// Total number of docs.                                 
       24 +    n_docs: u32,                                              
       25 +}                                                             
       26 +                                                              
       27 +impl Bm25 {                                                   
       28 +    pub fn build<I, S>(docs: I) -> Self                       
       29 +    where                                                     
       30 +        I: IntoIterator<Item = S>,                            
       31 +        S: AsRef<str>,                                        
       32 +    {                                                         
       33 +        let mut doc_lens: Vec<u32> = Vec::new();              
       34 +        let mut postings: HashMap<String, Vec<(u32, u32)>> = H
          +ashMap::new();                                                
       35 +                                                              
       36 +        for (i, doc) in docs.into_iter().enumerate() {        
       37 +            let tokens = tokenize(doc.as_ref());              
       38 +            doc_lens.push(tokens.len() as u32);               
       39 +                                                              
       40 +            let mut tf: HashMap<String, u32> = HashMap::new();
       41 +            for tok in tokens {                               
       42 +                *tf.entry(tok).or_insert(0) += 1;             
       43 +            }                                                 
       44 +            for (term, count) in tf {                         
       45 +                postings.entry(term).or_default().push((i as u
          +32, count));                                                  
       46 +            }                                                 
       47 +        }                                                     
       48 +                                                              
       49 +        let n_docs = doc_lens.len() as u32;                   
       50 +        let avg_doc_len = if n_docs == 0 {                    
       51 +            0.0                                               
       52 +        } else {                                              
       53 +            doc_lens.iter().map(|&l| l as f32).sum::<f32>() / 
          +n_docs as f32                                                 
       54 +        };                                                    
       55 +                                                              
       56 +        let idf: HashMap<String, f32> = postings              
       57 +            .iter()                                           
       58 +            .map(|(term, plist)| {                            
       59 +                let df = plist.len() as f32;                  
       60 +                let v = ((n_docs as f32 - df + 0.5) / (df + 0.
          +5) + 1.0).ln();                                               
       61 +                (term.clone(), v)                             
       62 +            })                                                
       63 +            .collect();                                       
       64 +                                                              
       65 +        Self {                                                
       66 +            doc_lens,                                         
       67 +            avg_doc_len,                                      
       68 +            postings,                                         
       69 +            idf,                                              
       70 +            n_docs,                                           
       71 +        }                                                     
       72 +    }                                                         
       73 +                                                              
       74 +    pub fn n_docs(&self) -> usize {                           
       75 +        self.n_docs as usize                                  
       76 +    }                                                         
       77 +                                                              
       78 +    /// Score every document against the query. Returns a Vec 
          +of length `n_docs`                                            
       79 +    /// where index i is the score for doc i. Mirrors `BM25Oka
          +pi.get_scores`.                                               
       80 +    pub fn scores(&self, query: &str) -> Vec<f32> {           
       81 +        let mut scores = vec![0.0f32; self.n_docs as usize];  
       82 +        if self.n_docs == 0 {                                 
       83 +            return scores;                                    
       84 +        }                                                     
       85 +        for term in tokenize(query) {                         
       86 +            let Some(idf) = self.idf.get(&term) else {        
       87 +                continue;                                     
       88 +            };                                                
       89 +            let Some(plist) = self.postings.get(&term) else { 
       90 +                continue;                                     
       91 +            };                                                
       92 +            for &(doc_idx, tf) in plist {                     
       93 +                let tf = tf as f32;                           
       94 +                let dl = self.doc_lens[doc_idx as usize] as f3
          +2;                                                            
       95 +                let denom = tf + K1 * (1.0 - B + B * dl / self
          +.avg_doc_len);                                                
       96 +                scores[doc_idx as usize] += idf * (tf * (K1 + 
          +1.0)) / denom;                                                
       97 +            }                                                 
       98 +        }                                                     
       99 +        scores                                                
      100 +    }                                                         
      101 +}                                                             
      102 +                                                              
      103 +pub fn tokenize(text: &str) -> Vec<String> {                  
      104 +    text.to_lowercase()                                       
      105 +        .split_whitespace()                                   
      106 +        .map(|s| s.to_string())                               
      107 +        .collect()                                            
      108 +}                                                             
      109 +                                                              
      110 +#[cfg(test)]                                                  
      111 +mod tests {                                                   
      112 +    use super::*;                                             
      113 +                                                              
      114 +    #[test]                                                   
      115 +    fn scores_match_python_reference() {                      
      116 +        // 3 docs, the same as a rank_bm25 example            
      117 +        let docs = ["the cat sat", "the dog ran", "cats and do
          +gs"];                                                         
      118 +        let bm = Bm25::build(docs);                           
      119 +        let s = bm.scores("cat");                             
      120 +        // doc 0 contains "cat", others don't вҶ’ only s[0] > 0 
      121 +        assert!(s[0] > 0.0);                                  
      122 +        assert_eq!(s[1], 0.0);                                
      123 +        assert_eq!(s[2], 0.0);                                
      124 +    }                                                         
      125 +                                                              
      126 +    #[test]                                                   
      127 +    fn empty_query_zero_scores() {                            
      128 +        let bm = Bm25::build(["a b c", "d e f"]);             
      129 +        let s = bm.scores("");                                
      130 +        assert_eq!(s, vec![0.0, 0.0]);                        
      131 +    }                                                         
      132 +                                                              
      133 +    #[test]                                                   
      134 +    fn unknown_term_zero_scores() {                           
      135 +        let bm = Bm25::build(["a b c", "d e f"]);             
      136 +        let s = bm.scores("zzz");                             
      137 +        assert_eq!(s, vec![0.0, 0.0]);                        
      138 +    }                                                         
      139 +}

       1 +//! Public engine API: `grep`, `semantic`, `hybrid`.           
       2 +                                                               
       3  pub mod generate;

       7 +use crate::models::{Chunk, SearchResult};                      
       8 +                                                               
       9 +#[derive(Debug, Clone)]                                        
      10 +pub struct Hit {                                               
      11 +    pub rank: usize,                                           
      12 +    pub result: SearchResult,                                  
      13 +}                                                              
      14 +                                                               
      15 +#[derive(Debug, Clone)]                                        
      16 +pub struct GrepResult {                                        
      17 +    pub query: String,                                         
      18 +    pub total_matches: usize,                                  
      19 +    pub hits: Vec<Hit>,                                        
      20 +}                                                              
      21 +                                                               
      22 +/// Case-insensitive substring search over chunks. Returns the 
         +top `n` matches                                                
      23 +/// plus the total match count. Mirrors `search_grep` in `src/r
         +agrep/search.py`.                                              
      24 +pub fn grep(                                                   
      25 +    chunks: &[Chunk],                                          
      26 +    term: &str,                                                
      27 +    source: Option<&str>,                                      
      28 +    n: usize,                                                  
      29 +) -> GrepResult {                                              
      30 +    let needle = term.to_lowercase();                          
      31 +    let filtered = chunks                                      
      32 +        .iter()                                                
      33 +        .filter(|c| source.map_or(true, |s| c.source == s))    
      34 +        .filter(|c| c.content.to_lowercase().contains(&needle))
         +;                                                              
      35 +                                                               
      36 +    let mut total = 0usize;                                    
      37 +    let mut hits = Vec::with_capacity(n);                      
      38 +    for c in filtered {                                        
      39 +        total += 1;                                            
      40 +        if hits.len() < n {                                    
      41 +            hits.push(Hit {                                    
      42 +                rank: hits.len() + 1,                          
      43 +                result: SearchResult {                         
      44 +                    chunk_id: c.id.clone(),                    
      45 +                    content: c.content.clone(),                
      46 +                    title: c.title.clone(),                    
      47 +                    source: c.source.clone(),                  
      48 +                    metadata: c.metadata.clone(),              
      49 +                    dense_score: 0.0,                          
      50 +                    bm25_score: 0.0,                           
      51 +                    rrf_score: 0.0,                            
      52 +                    rerank_score: 0.0,                         
      53 +                },                                             
      54 +            });                                                
      55 +        }                                                      
      56 +    }                                                          
      57 +                                                               
      58 +    GrepResult {                                               
      59 +        query: term.to_string(),                               
      60 +        total_matches: total,                                  
      61 +        hits,                                                  
      62 +    }                                                          
      63 +}

      101 +fn run_grep(dir: &std::path::Path, args: &SearchArgs) -> Resul
          +t<()> {                                                       
      102 +    if !store::chunks_exist(dir) {                            
      103 +        // Fall back to splash if the user has nothing to sear
          +ch.                                                           
      104 +        splash::print();                                      
      105 +        return Ok(());                                        
      106 +    }                                                         
      107 +                                                              
      108 +    let chunks = store::load_chunks(dir)?;                    
      109 +    let result = query::grep(&chunks, &args.term, args.source.
          +as_deref(), args.n);                                          
      110 +                                                              
      111 +    if args.json {                                            
      112 +        print_json(&result.query, "grep", Some(result.total_ma
          +tches), &result.hits, args)?;                                 
      113 +    } else {                                                  
      114 +        print_human(                                          
      115 +            &result.query,                                    
      116 +            "grep",                                           
      117 +            Some(result.total_matches),

      125 +fn print_human(                                               
      126 +    term: &str,                                               
      127 +    mode: &str,                                               
      128 +    total: Option<usize>,                                     
      129 +    hits: &[query::Hit],                                      
      130 +    args: &SearchArgs,                                        
      131 +) {                                                           
      132 +    if mode == "grep" {                                       
      133 +        if let Some(t) = total {                              
      134 +            println!("{} chunks match '{}'\n", t, term);      
      135 +        }                                                     
      136 +    } else {                                                  
      137 +        println!("Top {} results for '{}'\n", hits.len(), term
          +);                                                            
      138 +    }                                                         
      139 +    for h in hits {                                           
      140 +        let r = &h.result;                                    
      141 +        let score_str = scores_inline(r);                     
      142 +        println!("  [{}] [{}] {}  {}", h.rank, r.source, r.tit
          +le, score_str);                                               
      143 +        println!("      id: {}", r.chunk_id);                 
      144 +        if args.full {                                        
      145 +            println!("      {}", r.content);                  
      146 +        } else if args.context > 0 {                          
      147 +            println!("      {}", snippet(&r.content, args.cont
          +ext, term));                                                  
      148 +        }                                                     
      149 +    }                                                         
      150 +}                                                             
      151 +                                                              
      152 +fn scores_inline(r: &SearchResult) -> String {                
      153 +    let mut parts = Vec::new();                               
      154 +    if r.rerank_score != 0.0 {                                
      155 +        parts.push(format!("rerank={:.3}", r.rerank_score));  
      156 +    }                                                         
      157 +    if r.rrf_score != 0.0 {                                   
      158 +        parts.push(format!("rrf={:.3}", r.rrf_score));        
      159 +    }                                                         
      160 +    if r.dense_score != 0.0 {                                 
      161 +        parts.push(format!("dense={:.3}", r.dense_score));    
      162 +    }                                                         
      163 +    if r.bm25_score != 0.0 {                                  
      164 +        parts.push(format!("bm25={:.3}", r.bm25_score));      
      165 +    }                                                         
      166 +    parts.join("  ")                                          
      167 +}                                                             
      168 +                                                              
      169 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                          
      170 +struct JsonHit<'a> {                                          
      171 +    rank: usize,                                              
      172 +    id: &'a str,                                              
      173 +    source: &'a str,                                          
      174 +    title: String,                                            
      175 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      176 +    snippet: Option<String>,                                  
      177 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      178 +    content: Option<&'a str>,                                 
      179 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      180 +    rerank: Option<f32>,                                      
      181 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      182 +    rrf: Option<f32>,                                         
      183 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      184 +    dense: Option<f32>,                                       
      185 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      186 +    bm25: Option<f32>,                                        
      187 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      188 +    metadata: Option<&'a std::collections::BTreeMap<String, Me
          +taValue>>,                                                    
      189 +}                                                             
      190 +                                                              
      191 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                          
      192 +struct JsonOut<'a> {                                          
      193 +    query: &'a str,                                           
      194 +    mode: &'a str,                                            
      195 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      196 +    total_matches: Option<usize>,                             
      197 +    results: Vec<JsonHit<'a>>,                                
      198 +}                                                             
      199 +                                                              
      200 +fn print_json(                                                
      201 +    query: &str,                                              
      202 +    mode: &str,                                               
      203 +    total: Option<usize>,                                     
      204 +    hits: &[query::Hit],                                      
      205 +    args: &SearchArgs,                                        
      206 +) -> Result<()> {                                             
      207 +    let context = if args.json && !args.full && args.context =
          += 200 {                                                       
      208 +        // Mirror Python: in JSON mode, default to no snippet 
          +unless explicitly set.                                        
      209 +        0                                                     
      210 +    } else {                                                  
      211 +        args.context                                          
      212 +    };                                                        
      213 +                                                              
      214 +    let results: Vec<JsonHit> = hits                          
      215 +        .iter()                                               
      216 +        .map(|h| {                                            
      217 +            let r = &h.result;                                
      218 +            let title = if r.title.len() <= 80 {              
      219 +                r.title.clone()                               
      220 +            } else {                                          
      221 +                format!("{}...", &r.title[..77])              
      222 +            };                                                
      223 +            let (snippet_v, content_v) = if args.full {       
      224 +                (None, Some(r.content.as_str()))              
      225 +            } else if context > 0 {                           
      226 +                (Some(snippet(&r.content, context, query)), No
          +ne)                                                           
      227 +            } else {                                          
      228 +                (None, None)                                  
      229 +            };                                                
      230 +            JsonHit {                                         
      231 +                rank: h.rank,                                 
      232 +                id: r.chunk_id.as_str(),                      
      233 +                source: r.source.as_str(),                    
      234 +                title,                                        
      235 +                snippet: snippet_v,                           
      236 +                content: content_v,                           
      237 +                rerank: opt_score(r.rerank_score, args.scores)
          +,                                                             
      238 +                rrf: opt_score(r.rrf_score, args.scores),     
      239 +                dense: opt_score(r.dense_score, args.scores), 
      240 +                bm25: opt_score(r.bm25_score, args.scores),   
      241 +                metadata: if args.metadata { Some(&r.metadata)
          + } else { None },                                             
      242 +            }                                                 
      243 +        })                                                    
      244 +        .collect();                                           
      245 +                                                              
      246 +    let out = JsonOut {                                       
      247 +        query,                                                
      248 +        mode,                                                 
      249 +        total_matches: total,                                 
      250 +        results,                                              
      251 +    };                                                        
      252 +    println!("{}", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&out)?);      
      253 +    Ok(())                                                    
      254 +}                                                             
      255 +                                                              
      256 +fn opt_score(v: f32, on: bool) -> Option<f32> {               
      257 +    if on && v != 0.0 {                                       
      258 +        Some((v * 1000.0).round() / 1000.0)                   
      259 +    } else {                                                  
      260 +        None                                                  
      261 +    }                                                         
      262 +}                                                             
      263 +                                                              
      264 +fn snippet(content: &str, length: usize, term: &str) -> String
          + {                                                            
      265 +    let flat: String = content.chars().map(|c| if c == '\n' { 
          +' ' } else { c }).collect();                                  
      266 +    let trimmed = flat.trim();                                
      267 +    if length == 0 || length >= trimmed.chars().count() {     
      268 +        return trimmed.to_string();                           
      269 +    }                                                         
      270 +    let lower = trimmed.to_lowercase();                       
      271 +    if let Some(pos) = lower.find(&term.to_lowercase()) {     
      272 +        // Approximate centering on `term`. Convert byte pos t
          +o char pos.                                                   
      273 +        let prefix_chars = trimmed[..pos].chars().count();    
      274 +        let half_back = length / 4;                           
      275 +        let start = prefix_chars.saturating_sub(half_back);   
      276 +        let chars: Vec<char> = trimmed.chars().collect();     
      277 +        let end = (start + length).min(chars.len());          
      278 +        let mut s: String = chars[start..end].iter().collect()
          +;                                                             
      279 +        if start > 0 {                                        
      280 +            s.insert_str(0, "...");                           
      281 +        }                                                     
      282 +        if end < chars.len() {                                
      283 +            s.push_str("...");                                
      284 +        }                                                     
      285 +        return s;                                             
      286 +    }                                                         
      287 +    let chars: Vec<char> = trimmed.chars().collect();         
      288 +    let mut s: String = chars[..length.min(chars.len())].iter(
          +).collect();                                                  
      289 +    if chars.len() > length {                                 
      290 +        s.push_str("...");                                    
      291 +    }                                                         
      292 +    s                                                         
      293 +}

вҸә Write(rust/src/embed/voyage.rs)
  вҺҝ В Added 64 lines
       1 +//! Voyage AI embeddings вҖ” direct HTTP, no SDK.                
       2 +//!                                                            
       3 +//! Mirrors the post-`voyageai`-removal Python implementation i
         +n                                                              
       4 +//! `src/ragrep/ingest/embed.py::VoyageEmbedder` (httpx + retry
         +/backoff).                                                     
       5  
       6 +use std::env;                                                  
       7 +use std::time::Duration;                                       
       8 +                                                               
       9 +use anyhow::{anyhow, bail, Context, Result};                   
      10 +use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};                           
      11 +                                                               
      12 +const BASE: &str = "https://api.voyageai.com/v1";              
      13 +const ENV_KEY: &str = "VOYAGE_API_KEY";                        
      14 +const REQUEST_TIMEOUT: Duration = Duration::from_secs(30);     
      15 +                                                               
      16 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                           
      17 +struct EmbedRequest<'a> {                                      
      18 +    model: &'a str,                                            
      19 +    input: Vec<&'a str>,                                       
      20 +    input_type: &'a str,                                       
      21 +}                                                              
      22 +                                                               
      23 +#[derive(Deserialize)]                                         
      24 +struct EmbedResponse {                                         
      25 +    data: Vec<EmbedItem>,                                      
      26 +}                                                              
      27 +                                                               
      28 +#[derive(Deserialize)]                                         
      29 +struct EmbedItem {                                             
      30 +    embedding: Vec<f32>,                                       
      31 +    index: usize,                                              
      32 +}                                                              
      33 +                                                               
      34 +/// One-shot query embedding. Returns the L2-normalized 1024-d 
         +vector.                                                        
      35 +pub fn embed_query(model: &str, text: &str) -> Result<Vec<f32>>
         + {                                                             
      36 +    let key = env::var(ENV_KEY)                                
      37 +        .map_err(|_| anyhow!("{ENV_KEY} is not set (add to .env
         + or export it)"))?;                                            
      38 +    let client = reqwest::blocking::Client::builder()          
      39 +        .timeout(REQUEST_TIMEOUT)                              
      40 +        .build()                                               
      41 +        .context("building HTTP client")?;                     
      42 +    let resp = client                                          
      43 +        .post(format!("{BASE}/embeddings"))                    
      44 +        .bearer_auth(&key)                                     
      45 +        .json(&EmbedRequest {                                  
      46 +            model,                                             
      47 +            input: vec![text],                                 
      48 +            input_type: "query",                               
      49 +        })                                                     
      50 +        .send()                                                
      51 +        .context("sending embed request")?;                    
      52 +                                                               
      53 +    if !resp.status().is_success() {                           
      54 +        let status = resp.status();                            
      55 +        let body = resp.text().unwrap_or_default();            
      56 +        bail!("Voyage embed failed: HTTP {status} вҖ” {body}");  
      57 +    }                                                          
      58 +                                                               
      59 +    let mut payload: EmbedResponse = resp.json().context("parsi
         +ng embed response")?;                                          
      60 +    if payload.data.is_empty() {                               
      61 +        bail!("Voyage embed: empty data array");               
      62 +    }                                                          
      63 +    payload.data.sort_by_key(|x| x.index);                     
      64 +    Ok(payload.data.swap_remove(0).embedding)                  
      65 +}

       60 +                                                              
       61 +#[derive(Debug, Clone)]                                       
       62 +pub struct SemanticResult {                                   
       63 +    pub query: String,                                        
       64 +    pub hits: Vec<Hit>,                                       
       65 +}                                                             
       66 +                                                              
       67 +/// Dense vector search via mmapped flat index. Returns top `n
          +` hits with                                                   
       68 +/// `dense_score` populated. If `source` is set, fetches `n*3`
          + then post-filters.                                           
       69 +/// Mirrors `dense_search` in `src/ragrep/query/retrieve.py`. 
       70 +pub fn semantic(                                              
       71 +    flat: &Flat,                                              
       72 +    chunks: &[Chunk],                                         
       73 +    query: &str,                                              
       74 +    query_embedding: &[f32],                                  
       75 +    source: Option<&str>,                                     
       76 +    n: usize,                                                 
       77 +) -> SemanticResult {                                         
       78 +    let fetch_k = if source.is_some() { n * 3 } else { n };   
       79 +    let raw = flat.search(query_embedding, fetch_k);          
       80 +                                                              
       81 +    let mut hits = Vec::with_capacity(n);                     
       82 +    for (idx, score) in raw {                                 
       83 +        let chunk = &chunks[idx as usize];                    
       84 +        if let Some(s) = source {                             
       85 +            if chunk.source != s {                            
       86 +                continue;                                     
       87 +            }                                                 
       88 +        }                                                     
       89 +        hits.push(Hit {                                       
       90 +            rank: hits.len() + 1,                             
       91 +            result: SearchResult {                            
       92 +                chunk_id: chunk.id.clone(),                   
       93 +                content: chunk.content.clone(),               
       94 +                title: chunk.title.clone(),                   
       95 +                source: chunk.source.clone(),                 
       96 +                metadata: chunk.metadata.clone(),             
       97 +                dense_score: score,                           
       98 +                bm25_score: 0.0,                              
       99 +                rrf_score: 0.0,                               
      100 +                rerank_score: 0.0,                            
      101 +            },                                                
      102 +        });                                                   
      103 +        if hits.len() >= n {                                  
      104 +            break;                                            
      105 +        }                                                     
      106 +    }                                                         
      107 +                                                              
      108 +    SemanticResult {                                          
      109 +        query: query.to_string(),                             
      110 +        hits,                                                 
      111 +    }                                                         
      112 +}

вҸә Write(rust/src/query/retrieve.rs)
  вҺҝ В Added 99 lines
        1 +//! Hybrid retrieval primitives: dense + BM25 + RRF fusion.   
        2 +//!                                                           
        3 +//! Mirrors `src/ragrep/query/retrieve.py`.                   
        4  
        5 +use std::cmp::Ordering;                                       
        6 +use std::collections::{HashMap, HashSet};                     
        7 +                                                              
        8 +use crate::index::bm25::Bm25;                                 
        9 +use crate::index::flat::Flat;                                 
       10 +use crate::models::Chunk;                                     
       11 +                                                              
       12 +pub type Scored = (usize, f32);                               
       13 +                                                              
       14 +pub fn dense(                                                 
       15 +    flat: &Flat,                                              
       16 +    query_emb: &[f32],                                        
       17 +    chunks: &[Chunk],                                         
       18 +    top_k: usize,                                             
       19 +    source_filter: Option<&str>,                              
       20 +) -> Vec<Scored> {                                            
       21 +    let fetch_k = if source_filter.is_some() { top_k * 3 } els
          +e { top_k };                                                  
       22 +    flat.search(query_emb, fetch_k)                           
       23 +        .into_iter()                                          
       24 +        .filter(|(idx, _)| {                                  
       25 +            source_filter.is_none_or(|s| chunks[*idx as usize]
          +.source == s)                                                 
       26 +        })                                                    
       27 +        .take(top_k)                                          
       28 +        .map(|(idx, score)| (idx as usize, score))            
       29 +        .collect()                                            
       30 +}                                                             
       31 +                                                              
       32 +pub fn bm25(                                                  
       33 +    bm25: &Bm25,                                              
       34 +    chunks: &[Chunk],                                         
       35 +    query: &str,                                              
       36 +    top_k: usize,                                             
       37 +    source_filter: Option<&str>,                              
       38 +) -> Vec<Scored> {                                            
       39 +    let mut scores = bm25.scores(query);                      
       40 +    if let Some(s) = source_filter {                          
       41 +        for (i, c) in chunks.iter().enumerate() {             
       42 +            if c.source != s {                                
       43 +                scores[i] = 0.0;                              
       44 +            }                                                 
       45 +        }                                                     
       46 +    }                                                         
       47 +    let mut indexed: Vec<Scored> = scores                     
       48 +        .into_iter()                                          
       49 +        .enumerate()                                          
       50 +        .filter(|(_, s)| *s > 0.0)                            
       51 +        .collect();                                           
       52 +    let k = top_k.min(indexed.len());                         
       53 +    if k == 0 {                                               
       54 +        return Vec::new();                                    
       55 +    }                                                         
       56 +    indexed.select_nth_unstable_by(k - 1, |a, b| {            
       57 +        b.1.partial_cmp(&a.1).unwrap_or(Ordering::Equal)      
       58 +    });                                                       
       59 +    indexed.truncate(k);                                      
       60 +    indexed.sort_by(|a, b| b.1.partial_cmp(&a.1).unwrap_or(Ord
          +ering::Equal));                                               
       61 +    indexed                                                   
       62 +}                                                             
       63 +                                                              
       64 +/// (chunk_idx, dense_score, bm25_score, rrf_score) sorted by 
          +rrf_score desc.                                               
       65 +pub type Fused = (usize, f32, f32, f32);                      
       66 +                                                              
       67 +const MISSING_RANK: usize = 1000;                             
       68 +                                                              
       69 +pub fn rrf(dense_results: &[Scored], bm25_results: &[Scored], 
          +k: usize) -> Vec<Fused> {                                     
       70 +    let dense_ranks: HashMap<usize, usize> = dense_results    
       71 +        .iter()                                               
       72 +        .enumerate()                                          
       73 +        .map(|(rank, (idx, _))| (*idx, rank))                 
       74 +        .collect();                                           
       75 +    let bm25_ranks: HashMap<usize, usize> = bm25_results      
       76 +        .iter()                                               
       77 +        .enumerate()                                          
       78 +        .map(|(rank, (idx, _))| (*idx, rank))                 
       79 +        .collect();                                           
       80 +    let dense_scores: HashMap<usize, f32> = dense_results.iter
          +().copied().collect();                                        
       81 +    let bm25_scores: HashMap<usize, f32> = bm25_results.iter()
          +.copied().collect();                                          
       82 +                                                              
       83 +    let all: HashSet<usize> = dense_ranks.keys().chain(bm25_ra
          +nks.keys()).copied().collect();                               
       84 +                                                              
       85 +    let kf = k as f32;                                        
       86 +    let mut scored: Vec<Fused> = all                          
       87 +        .into_iter()                                          
       88 +        .map(|idx| {                                          
       89 +            let d_rank = dense_ranks.get(&idx).copied().unwrap
          +_or(MISSING_RANK);                                            
       90 +            let b_rank = bm25_ranks.get(&idx).copied().unwrap_
          +or(MISSING_RANK);                                             
       91 +            let rrf_score = 1.0 / (kf + d_rank as f32) + 1.0 /
          + (kf + b_rank as f32);                                        
       92 +            let d = dense_scores.get(&idx).copied().unwrap_or(
          +0.0);                                                         
       93 +            let b = bm25_scores.get(&idx).copied().unwrap_or(0
          +.0);                                                          
       94 +            (idx, d, b, rrf_score)                            
       95 +        })                                                    
       96 +        .collect();                                           
       97 +                                                              
       98 +    scored.sort_by(|a, b| b.3.partial_cmp(&a.3).unwrap_or(Orde
          +ring::Equal));                                                
       99 +    scored                                                    
      100 +}

      115 +#[derive(Debug, Clone)]                                       
      116 +pub struct HybridResult {                                     
      117 +    pub query: String,                                        
      118 +    pub hits: Vec<Hit>,                                       
      119 +}                                                             
      120 +                                                              
      121 +pub struct HybridOpts<'a> {                                   
      122 +    pub n: usize,                                             
      123 +    pub top_k_dense: usize,                                   
      124 +    pub top_k_bm25: usize,                                    
      125 +    pub rrf_k: usize,                                         
      126 +    pub rerank_provider: &'a str,                             
      127 +    pub rerank_model: &'a str,                                
      128 +    pub source: Option<&'a str>,                              
      129 +}                                                             
      130 +                                                              
      131 +/// Hybrid retrieval: dense + BM25 вҶ’ RRF fusion вҶ’ rerank top-`
          +n`.                                                           
      132 +/// Mirrors `retrieve()` + Voyage rerank from `src/ragrep/quer
          +y/`.                                                          
      133 +pub fn hybrid(                                                
      134 +    flat: &Flat,                                              
      135 +    bm25_idx: &Bm25,                                          
      136 +    chunks: &[Chunk],                                         
      137 +    query: &str,                                              
      138 +    query_embedding: &[f32],                                  
      139 +    opts: HybridOpts<'_>,                                     
      140 +) -> anyhow::Result<HybridResult> {                           
      141 +    let dense_hits = retrieve::dense(flat, query_embedding, ch
          +unks, opts.top_k_dense, opts.source);                         
      142 +    let bm25_hits = retrieve::bm25(bm25_idx, chunks, query, op
          +ts.top_k_bm25, opts.source);                                  
      143 +    let fused = retrieve::rrf(&dense_hits, &bm25_hits, opts.rr
          +f_k);                                                         
      144 +                                                              
      145 +    let pre_n = opts.n.min(fused.len());                      
      146 +    let pre = &fused[..pre_n];                                
      147 +    let docs: Vec<&str> = pre                                 
      148 +        .iter()                                               
      149 +        .map(|(idx, _, _, _)| chunks[*idx].content.as_str())  
      150 +        .collect();                                           
      151 +                                                              
      152 +    let rerank_items =                                        
      153 +        rerank::rerank(opts.rerank_provider, opts.rerank_model
          +, query, &docs, opts.n)?;                                     
      154 +                                                              
      155 +    let mut hits = Vec::with_capacity(rerank_items.len());    
      156 +    for (rank, item) in rerank_items.into_iter().enumerate() {
      157 +        let (idx, dense, bm25_s, rrf_s) = pre[item.index];    
      158 +        let chunk = &chunks[idx];                             
      159 +        hits.push(Hit {                                       
      160 +            rank: rank + 1,                                   
      161 +            result: SearchResult {                            
      162 +                chunk_id: chunk.id.clone(),                   
      163 +                content: chunk.content.clone(),               
      164 +                title: chunk.title.clone(),                   
      165 +                source: chunk.source.clone(),                 
      166 +                metadata: chunk.metadata.clone(),             
      167 +                dense_score: dense,                           
      168 +                bm25_score: bm25_s,                           
      169 +                rrf_score: rrf_s,                             
      170 +                rerank_score: item.score,                     
      171 +            },                                                
      172 +        });                                                   
      173 +    }                                                         
      174 +                                                              
      175 +    Ok(HybridResult {                                         
      176 +        query: query.to_string(),                             
      177 +        hits,                                                 
      178 +    })                                                        
      179 +}

  Binary grew from 773KB вҶ’ 4.6MB now that reqwest+rustls+axum+yup-oauth2+git2
  are linked (git2 vendors libgit2 = ~2MB on its own).

  Phase 1 ship-gate вң“: the binary is usable end-to-end against the existing
  Python-built index. We're at v0.2.0-rust-able state.

  Outstanding from Phase 1 plan:
  1. cli::search::proxy (server mode): --server URL proxies to HTTP /search,
  with Cloud Run identity-token auth. ~1 day. Needed before users on Cloud Run
  can use the Rust binary.
  2. Pre-warm rayon (polish): hides ~6ms first-call rayon init. Trivial change.
  3. Broader parity test (50 queries): the plan asks for a tools/parity.sh that
  runs 50 queries through Python and Rust and confirms вүҘ9/10 top-10 overlap.
  Validates we haven't drifted on edge cases.

  I'd do them in this order: (3) parity.sh first to catch any latent
  divergences, then (1) server proxy to unlock real-world deployment, then (2)
  pre-warm as a quick last polish.

  Or вҖ” Phase 1 is done enough to switch context to Phase 2 (the ingest pipeline:
   chunking, scrapers' normalize step, full embed batching with throttle) which
  is much bigger.

  What's next?

      115 +fn run_proxy(server: &str, args: &SearchArgs) -> Result<()> { 
      116 +    use std::time::Duration;                                  
      117 +                                                              
      118 +    let url = format!("{}/search", server.trim_end_matches('/'
          +));                                                           
      119 +    let client = reqwest::blocking::Client::builder()         
      120 +        .timeout(Duration::from_secs(180))                    
      121 +        .build()                                              
      122 +        .context("building HTTP client")?;                    
      123 +                                                              
      124 +    let n_str = args.n.to_string();                           
      125 +    let context_str = args.context.to_string();               
      126 +    let full_str = args.full.to_string();                     
      127 +    let scores_str = args.scores.to_string();                 
      128 +    let metadata_str = args.metadata.to_string();             
      129 +    let mut params: Vec<(&str, &str)> = vec![                 
      130 +        ("q", args.term.as_str()),                            
      131 +        ("mode", &args.mode),                                 
      132 +        ("n", &n_str),                                        
      133 +        ("context", &context_str),                            
      134 +        ("full", &full_str),                                  
      135 +        ("scores", &scores_str),                              
      136 +        ("metadata", &metadata_str),                          
      137 +    ];                                                        
      138 +    if let Some(s) = args.source.as_deref() {                 
      139 +        params.push(("source", s));                           
      140 +    }                                                         
      141 +                                                              
      142 +    let resp = client                                         
      143 +        .get(&url)                                            
      144 +        .query(&params)                                       
      145 +        .send()                                               
      146 +        .with_context(|| format!("contacting server at {server
          +}"))?;                                                        
      147 +                                                              
      148 +    if !resp.status().is_success() {                          
      149 +        let status = resp.status();                           
      150 +        let body = resp.text().unwrap_or_default();           
      151 +        bail!("server returned {status}: {body}");            
      152 +    }                                                         
      153 +    let body = resp.text().context("reading server response bo
          +dy")?;                                                        
      154 +                                                              
      155 +    if args.json {                                            
      156 +        println!("{body}");                                   
      157 +        return Ok(());                                        
      158 +    }                                                         
      159 +                                                              
      160 +    let payload: ServerPayload =                              
      161 +        serde_json::from_str(&body).context("parsing server re
          +sponse (expected JSON)")?;                                    
      162 +                                                              
      163 +    if payload.mode == "grep" {                               
      164 +        if let Some(t) = payload.total_matches {              
      165 +            println!("{} chunks match '{}'\n", t, args.term); 
      166 +        }                                                     
      167 +    } else {                                                  
      168 +        println!("Top {} results for '{}'\n", payload.results.
          +len(), args.term);                                            
      169 +    }                                                         
      170 +    for r in &payload.results {                               
      171 +        let score_str = if args.scores { server_scores_inline(
          +r) } else { String::new() };                                  
      172 +        println!(                                             
      173 +            "  [{}] [{}] {}  {}",                             
      174 +            r.rank,                                           
      175 +            r.source,                                         
      176 +            truncate_title(&r.title),                         
      177 +            score_str                                         
      178 +        );                                                    
      179 +        println!("      id: {}", r.id);                       
      180 +        if let Some(c) = &r.content {                         
      181 +            println!("      {}", c);                          
      182 +        } else if let Some(s) = &r.snippet {                  
      183 +            println!("      {}", s);                          
      184 +        }                                                     
      185 +    }                                                         
      186 +    Ok(())                                                    
      187 +}                                                             
      188 +                                                              
      189 +#[derive(serde::Deserialize)]                                 
      190 +struct ServerPayload {                                        
      191 +    mode: String,                                             
      192 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
      193 +    total_matches: Option<usize>,                             
      194 +    results: Vec<ServerResult>,                               
      195 +}                                                             
      196 +                                                              
      197 +#[derive(serde::Deserialize)]                                 
      198 +struct ServerResult {                                         
      199 +    rank: usize,                                              
      200 +    id: String,                                               
      201 +    source: String,                                           
      202 +    title: String,                                            
      203 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
      204 +    snippet: Option<String>,                                  
      205 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
      206 +    content: Option<String>,                                  
      207 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
      208 +    rerank: Option<f32>,                                      
      209 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
      210 +    rrf: Option<f32>,                                         
      211 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
      212 +    dense: Option<f32>,                                       
      213 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
      214 +    bm25: Option<f32>,                                        
      215 +}                                                             
      216 +                                                              
      217 +fn server_scores_inline(r: &ServerResult) -> String {         
      218 +    let mut parts = Vec::new();                               
      219 +    if let Some(v) = r.rerank {                               
      220 +        parts.push(format!("rerank={v:.3}"));                 
      221 +    }                                                         
      222 +    if let Some(v) = r.rrf {                                  
      223 +        parts.push(format!("rrf={v:.3}"));                    
      224 +    }                                                         
      225 +    if let Some(v) = r.dense {                                
      226 +        parts.push(format!("dense={v:.3}"));                  
      227 +    }                                                         
      228 +    if let Some(v) = r.bm25 {                                 
      229 +        parts.push(format!("bm25={v:.3}"));                   
      230 +    }                                                         
      231 +    parts.join("  ")                                          
      232 +}
