        1 +//! Recursive token-based document chunking.                  
        2 +//!                                                           
        3 +//! Direct port of `src/ragrep/ingest/chunk.py`. The token est
          +imator is a                                                   
        4 +//! heuristic вҖ” `max(word_count, len_bytes/4)` вҖ” chosen over a
          + real                                                         
        5 +//! tokenizer (tiktoken etc.) because it handles tab-delimited
          + content like                                                 
        6 +//! CSV exports and code where real tokenizers underestimate. 
        7  
        8 +use crate::models::{Chunk, Document, MetaValue};              
        9 +                                                              
       10 +/// Sources that are typically small and never get split.     
       11 +const NO_CHUNK_SOURCES: &[&str] = &["bookmark", "pin"];       
       12 +                                                              
       13 +/// Separators in priority order for recursive splitting.     
       14 +const SEPARATORS: &[&str] = &["\n\n", "\n", "\t", ". ", " "]; 
       15 +                                                              
       16 +/// Hard byte limit per chunk (safety valve; ~1K tokens at ~4 
          +bytes/token).                                                 
       17 +const MAX_BYTES: usize = 4000;                                
       18 +                                                              
       19 +/// Heuristic token count: max(word_count, byte_len / 4). The 
          +byte/4 fallback                                               
       20 +/// catches tab-delimited content and dense code where word_co
          +unt                                                           
       21 +/// underestimates token cost.                                
       22 +fn approx_tokens(text: &str) -> usize {                       
       23 +    let words = text.split_whitespace().count();              
       24 +    let bytes_4 = text.len() / 4;                             
       25 +    words.max(bytes_4)                                        
       26 +}                                                             
       27 +                                                              
       28 +/// Recursively split `text` into chunks under `max_tokens`. W
          +alks                                                          
       29 +/// SEPARATORS in priority order, falling back to a hard word-
          +count split                                                   
       30 +/// if no separator yields multiple parts.                    
       31 +fn recursive_split(text: &str, max_tokens: usize, overlap_toke
          +ns: usize) -> Vec<String> {                                   
       32 +    if approx_tokens(text) <= max_tokens {                    
       33 +        return vec![text.to_string()];                        
       34 +    }                                                         
       35 +                                                              
       36 +    for sep in SEPARATORS {                                   
       37 +        let parts: Vec<&str> = text.split(sep).collect();     
       38 +        if parts.len() <= 1 {                                 
       39 +            continue;                                         
       40 +        }                                                     
       41 +                                                              
       42 +        let mut chunks: Vec<String> = Vec::new();             
       43 +        let mut current = parts[0].to_string();               
       44 +                                                              
       45 +        for part in &parts[1..] {                             
       46 +            let candidate = format!("{current}{sep}{part}");  
       47 +            if approx_tokens(&candidate) <= max_tokens {      
       48 +                current = candidate;                          
       49 +            } else {                                          
       50 +                let trimmed = current.trim();                 
       51 +                if !trimmed.is_empty() {                      
       52 +                    chunks.push(trimmed.to_string());         
       53 +                }                                             
       54 +                if overlap_tokens > 0 {                       
       55 +                    let words: Vec<&str> = current.split_white
          +space().collect();                                            
       56 +                    let take = overlap_tokens.min(words.len())
          +;                                                             
       57 +                    let tail = words[words.len() - take..].joi
          +n(" ");                                                       
       58 +                    if tail.is_empty() {                      
       59 +                        current = (*part).to_string();        
       60 +                    } else {                                  
       61 +                        current = format!("{tail}{sep}{part}")
          +.trim().to_string();                                          
       62 +                    }                                         
       63 +                } else {                                      
       64 +                    current = (*part).to_string();            
       65 +                }                                             
       66 +            }                                                 
       67 +        }                                                     
       68 +                                                              
       69 +        let trimmed = current.trim();                         
       70 +        if !trimmed.is_empty() {                              
       71 +            chunks.push(trimmed.to_string());                 
       72 +        }                                                     
       73 +                                                              
       74 +        if chunks.len() > 1 {                                 
       75 +            return chunks;                                    
       76 +        }                                                     
       77 +    }                                                         
       78 +                                                              
       79 +    // Final fallback: hard split by words at max_tokens.     
       80 +    let words: Vec<&str> = text.split_whitespace().collect(); 
       81 +    let stride = max_tokens.saturating_sub(overlap_tokens).max
          +(1);                                                          
       82 +    let mut chunks = Vec::new();                              
       83 +    let mut i = 0;                                            
       84 +    while i < words.len() {                                   
       85 +        let end = (i + max_tokens).min(words.len());          
       86 +        let piece = words[i..end].join(" ");                  
       87 +        let trimmed = piece.trim();                           
       88 +        if !trimmed.is_empty() {                              
       89 +            chunks.push(trimmed.to_string());                 
       90 +        }                                                     
       91 +        if end == words.len() {                               
       92 +            break;                                            
       93 +        }                                                     
       94 +        i += stride;                                          
       95 +    }                                                         
       96 +    chunks                                                    
       97 +}                                                             
       98 +                                                              
       99 +fn make_id(doc_id: &str, idx: usize) -> String {              
      100 +    format!("{doc_id}:{idx}")                                 
      101 +}                                                             
      102 +                                                              
      103 +fn metadata_with_chunk_idx(                                   
      104 +    base: &std::collections::BTreeMap<String, MetaValue>,     
      105 +    idx: usize,                                               
      106 +) -> std::collections::BTreeMap<String, MetaValue> {          
      107 +    let mut m = base.clone();                                 
      108 +    m.insert("chunk_idx".to_string(), MetaValue::Int(idx as i6
          +4));                                                          
      109 +    m                                                         
      110 +}                                                             
      111 +                                                              
      112 +pub fn chunk_document(doc: &Document, max_tokens: usize, overl
          +ap_tokens: usize) -> Vec<Chunk> {                             
      113 +    if NO_CHUNK_SOURCES.contains(&doc.source.as_str()) || appr
          +ox_tokens(&doc.content) <= max_tokens {                       
      114 +        return vec![Chunk {                                   
      115 +            id: make_id(&doc.id, 0),                          
      116 +            doc_id: doc.id.clone(),                           
      117 +            content: doc.content.clone(),                     
      118 +            title: doc.title.clone(),                         
      119 +            source: doc.source.clone(),                       
      120 +            metadata: metadata_with_chunk_idx(&doc.metadata, 0
          +),                                                            
      121 +        }];                                                   
      122 +    }                                                         
      123 +                                                              
      124 +    let parts = recursive_split(&doc.content, max_tokens, over
          +lap_tokens);                                                  
      125 +                                                              
      126 +    // Safety valve: split by byte length when any single part
          + exceeds MAX_BYTES.                                           
      127 +    let mut safe: Vec<String> = Vec::new();                   
      128 +    for part in parts {                                       
      129 +        if part.len() <= MAX_BYTES {                          
      130 +            safe.push(part);                                  
      131 +        } else {                                              
      132 +            // Walk char boundaries to avoid splitting a multi
          +byte sequence.                                                
      133 +            let bytes = part.as_bytes();                      
      134 +            let mut start = 0;                                
      135 +            while start < bytes.len() {                       
      136 +                let mut end = (start + MAX_BYTES).min(bytes.le
          +n());                                                         
      137 +                while end < bytes.len() && (bytes[end] & 0b110
          +0_0000) == 0b1000_0000 {                                      
      138 +                    end -= 1;                                 
      139 +                }                                             
      140 +                let segment = part[start..end].trim();        
      141 +                if !segment.is_empty() {                      
      142 +                    safe.push(segment.to_string());           
      143 +                }                                             
      144 +                start = end;                                  
      145 +            }                                                 
      146 +        }                                                     
      147 +    }                                                         
      148 +                                                              
      149 +    safe.into_iter()                                          
      150 +        .enumerate()                                          
      151 +        .map(|(i, content)| Chunk {                           
      152 +            id: make_id(&doc.id, i),                          
      153 +            doc_id: doc.id.clone(),                           
      154 +            content,                                          
      155 +            title: doc.title.clone(),                         
      156 +            source: doc.source.clone(),                       
      157 +            metadata: metadata_with_chunk_idx(&doc.metadata, i
          +),                                                            
      158 +        })                                                    
      159 +        .collect()                                            
      160 +}                                                             
      161 +                                                              
      162 +pub fn all(docs: &[Document], max_tokens: usize, overlap_token
          +s: usize) -> Vec<Chunk> {                                     
      163 +    let mut out: Vec<Chunk> = Vec::new();                     
      164 +    for doc in docs {                                         
      165 +        out.extend(chunk_document(doc, max_tokens, overlap_tok
          +ens));                                                        
      166 +    }                                                         
      167 +    out                                                       
      168 +}                                                             
      169 +

      171 +mod tests {                                                   
      172 +    use super::*;                                             
      173 +    use std::collections::BTreeMap;                           
      174 +                                                              
      175 +    fn doc(id: &str, source: &str, content: &str) -> Document 
          +{

      177 +            id: id.into(),                                    
      178 +            source: source.into(),

      185 +    #[test]                                                   
      186 +    fn small_doc_yields_single_chunk() {                      
      187 +        let d = doc("d1", "slack", "short message");          
      188 +        let chunks = chunk_document(&d, 512, 64);             
      189 +        assert_eq!(chunks.len(), 1);                          
      190 +        assert_eq!(chunks[0].id, "d1:0");                     
      191 +        assert_eq!(chunks[0].content, "short message");       
      192 +        assert!(matches!(chunks[0].metadata.get("chunk_idx"), 
          +Some(MetaValue::Int(0))));                                    
      193 +    }                                                         
      194 +                                                              
      195 +    #[test]                                                   
      196 +    fn no_chunk_sources_never_split() {                       
      197 +        let big = "x ".repeat(5000); // 10000 chars, far over 
          +max_tokens                                                    
      198 +        let d = doc("d1", "bookmark", &big);                  
      199 +        let chunks = chunk_document(&d, 512, 64);             
      200 +        assert_eq!(chunks.len(), 1);                          
      201 +        assert_eq!(chunks[0].source, "bookmark");             
      202 +    }                                                         
      203 +                                                              
      204 +    #[test]                                                   
      205 +    fn long_doc_splits_at_paragraph() {                       
      206 +        let para = "word ".repeat(300); // ~300 tokens        
      207 +        let content = format!("{para}\n\n{para}\n\n{para}");  
      208 +        let d = doc("d1", "slack", &content);                 
      209 +        let chunks = chunk_document(&d, 512, 0);              
      210 +        assert!(chunks.len() >= 2, "got {} chunks", chunks.len
          +());                                                          
      211 +        for (i, c) in chunks.iter().enumerate() {             
      212 +            assert_eq!(c.id, format!("d1:{i}"));              
      213 +            assert!(matches!(c.metadata.get("chunk_idx"), Some
          +(MetaValue::Int(n)) if *n == i as i64));                      
      214 +        }                                                     
      215 +    }                                                         
      216 +                                                              
      217 +    #[test]                                                   
      218 +    fn approx_tokens_uses_byte_max_for_dense_content() {      
      219 +        // 10 words but 1000 bytes (CSV-style): byte/4 = 250 d
          +ominates.                                                     
      220 +        let dense = "a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h,i,j,".repeat(50);        
      221 +        assert!(approx_tokens(&dense) > 50);                  
      222 +    }                                                         
      223 +                                                              
      224 +    #[test]                                                   
      225 +    fn overlap_carries_tail_words() {                         
      226 +        let para = "alpha beta gamma delta epsilon zeta eta th
          +eta ".repeat(50);                                             
      227 +        let content = format!("{para}\n{para}");              
      228 +        let d = doc("d1", "slack", &content);                 
      229 +        let chunks = chunk_document(&d, 64, 8);               
      230 +        assert!(chunks.len() >= 2);                           
      231 +        // The second chunk should start with words drawn from
          + the tail of the first.                                       
      232 +        if chunks.len() >= 2 {                                
      233 +            let first_tail: Vec<&str> = chunks[0].content.spli
          +t_whitespace().rev().take(8).collect();                       
      234 +            let second_head: Vec<&str> = chunks[1].content.spl
          +it_whitespace().take(8).collect();                            
      235 +            // At least one of the trailing words from chunk 0
          + should appear in                                             
      236 +            // the first 16 words of chunk 1 (overlap may stra
          +ddle separator).                                              
      237 +            let any_overlap = first_tail.iter().any(|w| second
          +_head.contains(w));                                           
      238 +            assert!(any_overlap, "no overlap; first tail={firs
          +t_tail:?} second head={second_head:?}");                      
      239 +        }                                                     
      240 +    }                                                         
      241 +}

        1 +//! Source-specific normalizers: raw JSONL вҶ’ `Document`.      
        2 +//!

          +eads one source's

       52 +pub fn read_jsonl(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<Value>> {        
       53 +    if !path.exists() {                                       
       54 +        return Ok(Vec::new());                                
       55 +    }                                                         
       56 +    let f = File::open(path).with_context(|| format!("opening 
          +{}", path.display()))?;                                       
       57 +    let r = BufReader::new(f);                                
       58 +    let mut out = Vec::new();                                 
       59 +    for (i, line) in r.lines().enumerate() {                  
       60 +        let line = line.with_context(|| format!("reading line 
          +{} of {}", i + 1, path.display()))?;                          
       61 +        let s = line.trim();                                  
       62 +        if s.is_empty() {                                     
       63 +            continue;                                         
       64 +        }                                                     
       65 +        let v: Value = serde_json::from_str(s)                
       66 +            .with_context(|| format!("parsing JSON on line {} 
          +of {}", i + 1, path.display()))?;                             
       67 +        out.push(v);                                          
       68 +    }                                                         
       69 +    Ok(out)                                                   
       70 +}                                                             
       71 +                                                              
       72 +pub fn load_users(path: &Path) -> Result<UserMap> {           
       73 +    if !path.exists() {                                       
       74 +        return Ok(HashMap::new());                            
       75 +    }                                                         
       76 +    let raw = std::fs::read_to_string(path).with_context(|| fo
          +rmat!("reading {}", path.display()))?;                        
       77 +    let v: Value = serde_json::from_str(&raw).with_context(|| 
          +format!("parsing {}", path.display()))?;                      
       78 +    let mut out = HashMap::new();                             
       79 +    match v {                                                 
       80 +        Value::Array(arr) => {                                
       81 +            for item in arr {                                 
       82 +                if let Some(id) = item.get("id").and_then(|v| 
          +v.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string()) {                          
       83 +                    let info: UserInfo = serde_json::from_valu
          +e(item).unwrap_or_default();                                  
       84 +                    out.insert(id, info);                     
       85 +                }                                             
       86 +            }                                                 
       87 +        }                                                     
       88 +        Value::Object(map) => {                               
       89 +            for (k, v) in map {                               
       90 +                let info: UserInfo = serde_json::from_value(v)
          +.unwrap_or_default();                                         
       91 +                out.insert(k, info);                          
       92 +            }                                                 
       93 +        }                                                     
       94 +        _ => {}                                               
       95 +    }                                                         
       96 +    Ok(out)                                                   
       97 +}

      126 +// Compiled-once regex patterns for slack mrkdwn cleaning.    
      127 +// Matches the 10 patterns at the top of `normalize.py`.      
      128 +                                                              
      129 +macro_rules! re {                                             
      130 +    ($name:ident, $pattern:expr) => {                         
      131 +        fn $name() -> &'static Regex {                        
      132 +            static R: OnceLock<Regex> = OnceLock::new();      
      133 +            R.get_or_init(|| Regex::new($pattern).unwrap())   
      134 +        }                                                     
      135 +    };                                                        
      136 +}                                                             
      137 +                                                              
      138 +re!(channel_link_re, r"<#\w+\|([^>]+)>");                     
      139 +re!(labeled_link_re, r"<(https?://[^|>]+)\|([^>]+)>");        
      140 +re!(bare_link_re, r"<(https?://[^>]+)>");                     
      141 +re!(user_mention_re, r"<@(\w+)>");                            
      142 +re!(emoji_re, r":[\w+\-]+:");                                 
      143 +re!(bold_re, r"\*([^*]+)\*");                                 
      144 +re!(italic_re, r"_([^_]+)_");                                 
      145 +re!(strike_re, r"~([^~]+)~");                                 
      146 +re!(mailto_re, r"<mailto:([^|>]+)\|([^>]+)>");                
      147 +re!(tel_re, r"<tel:([^|>]+)\|([^>]+)>");                      
      148 +re!(spaces_re, r"[ \t]+");                                    
      149 +                                                              
      150 +pub fn clean_text(text: &str, users: &UserMap) -> String {    
      151 +    let mut s = text.to_string();                             
      152 +    s = user_mention_re()                                     
      153 +        .replace_all(&s, |caps: &regex::Captures| {           
      154 +            let id = &caps[1];                                
      155 +            let name = users                                  
      156 +                .get(id)                                      
      157 +                .map(|u| u.name.as_str())                     
      158 +                .filter(|n| !n.is_empty())                    
      159 +                .unwrap_or(id);                               
      160 +            format!("@{name}")                                
      161 +        })                                                    
      162 +        .into_owned();                                        
      163 +    s = mailto_re().replace_all(&s, "$2").into_owned();       
      164 +    s = tel_re().replace_all(&s, "$2").into_owned();          
      165 +    s = channel_link_re().replace_all(&s, "#$1").into_owned();
      166 +    s = labeled_link_re().replace_all(&s, "$2").into_owned(); 
      167 +    s = bare_link_re().replace_all(&s, "$1").into_owned();    
      168 +    s = emoji_re().replace_all(&s, "").into_owned();          
      169 +    s = bold_re().replace_all(&s, "$1").into_owned();         
      170 +    s = italic_re().replace_all(&s, "$1").into_owned();       
      171 +    s = strike_re().replace_all(&s, "$1").into_owned();       
      172 +    s = spaces_re().replace_all(&s, " ").into_owned();        
      173 +    s.trim().to_string()                                      
      174 +}

      176 +pub fn user_label(uid: &str, users: &UserMap) -> String {     
      177 +    match users.get(uid) {                                    
      178 +        Some(u) if !u.title.is_empty() => format!("{} ({})", u
          +.name, u.title),                                              
      179 +        Some(u) if !u.name.is_empty() => u.name.clone(),      
      180 +        _ => uid.to_string(),                                 
      181 +    }                                                         
      182 +}

      184 +/// Short stable hash for synthesizing IDs (12 hex chars from 
          +sha256).                                                      
      185 +pub fn short_hash(s: &str) -> String {                        
      186 +    let h = Sha256::digest(s.as_bytes());                     
      187 +    let mut out = String::with_capacity(12);                  
      188 +    for b in &h[..6] {                                        
      189 +        use std::fmt::Write;                                  
      190 +        let _ = write!(out, "{b:02x}");                       
      191 +    }                                                         
      192 +    out                                                       
      193 +}

      195 +/// Normalize all sources from `raw_dir` and dedup by `Documen
          +t.id`.                                                        
      196 +pub fn normalize_all(raw_dir: &Path) -> Result<Vec<Document>> 
          +{                                                             
      197 +    let users = load_users(&raw_dir.join("users.json"))?;     
      198 +    let channels = load_channels(&raw_dir.join("channels.json"
          +))?;                                                          
      199 +                                                              
      200 +    let mut docs: Vec<Document> = Vec::new();                 
      201 +    docs.extend(slack::normalize(raw_dir, &users, &channels)?)
          +;                                                             
      202 +    docs.extend(atlassian::normalize(raw_dir)?);              
      203 +    docs.extend(gdrive::normalize(raw_dir)?);                 
      204 +    docs.extend(git::normalize(raw_dir)?);                    
      205 +    docs.extend(file::normalize(raw_dir)?);                   
      206 +    docs.extend(bookmark::normalize(raw_dir)?);               
      207 +    docs.extend(pin::normalize(raw_dir, &users)?);            
      208 +    docs.extend(bitbucket::normalize(raw_dir)?);              
      209 +    docs.extend(code::normalize(raw_dir)?);                   
      210 +                                                              
      211 +    let mut seen: HashSet<String> = HashSet::with_capacity(doc
          +s.len());                                                     
      212 +    docs.retain(|d| seen.insert(d.id.clone()));               
      213 +    Ok(docs)                                                  
      214 +}                                                             
      215 +                                                              
      216 +#[cfg(test)]                                                  
      217 +mod tests {                                                   
      218 +    use super::*;                                             
      219 +                                                              
      220 +    fn users() -> UserMap {                                   
      221 +        let mut m = HashMap::new();                           
      222 +        m.insert(                                             
      223 +            "U123".into(),                                    
      224 +            UserInfo {                                        
      225 +                name: "alice".into(),                         
      226 +                title: "engineer".into(),                     
      227 +            },                                                
      228 +        );                                                    
      229 +        m                                                     
      230 +    }                                                         
      231 +                                                              
      232 +    #[test]                                                   
      233 +    fn user_label_with_title() {                              
      234 +        assert_eq!(user_label("U123", &users()), "alice (engin
          +eer)");                                                       
      235 +    }                                                         
      236 +                                                              
      237 +    #[test]                                                   
      238 +    fn user_label_unknown_falls_back_to_id() {                
      239 +        assert_eq!(user_label("U999", &users()), "U999");     
      240 +    }                                                         
      241 +                                                              
      242 +    #[test]                                                   
      243 +    fn clean_text_strips_mrkdwn() {                           
      244 +        let txt = "Hi <@U123>, see <https://example.com|the do
          +cs> *now* :smile:";                                           
      245 +        let cleaned = clean_text(txt, &users());              
      246 +        assert_eq!(cleaned, "Hi @alice, see the docs now");   
      247 +    }                                                         
      248 +                                                              
      249 +    #[test]                                                   
      250 +    fn clean_text_strips_channel_link_and_emoji_and_bold_and_i
          +talic() {                                                     
      251 +        let txt = "*bold* _italic_ ~strike~ in <#C1|general> :
          +emoji:";                                                      
      252 +        let cleaned = clean_text(txt, &HashMap::new());       
      253 +        assert_eq!(cleaned, "bold italic strike in #general");
      254 +    }                                                         
      255 +                                                              
      256 +    #[test]                                                   
      257 +    fn clean_text_collapses_whitespace() {                    
      258 +        let txt = "a    b\tc";                                
      259 +        let cleaned = clean_text(txt, &HashMap::new());       
      260 +        assert_eq!(cleaned, "a b c");                         
      261 +    }                                                         
      262 +                                                              
      263 +    #[test]                                                   
      264 +    fn short_hash_is_stable_and_12_chars() {                  
      265 +        let a = short_hash("hello");                          
      266 +        let b = short_hash("hello");                          
      267 +        assert_eq!(a, b);                                     
      268 +        assert_eq!(a.len(), 12);                              
      269 +        assert_ne!(short_hash("hello"), short_hash("world")); 
      270 +    }

       1 +//! Extracted file content (PDF/DOCX/PPTX/XLSX вҶ’ text) вҶ’ Docume
         +nt.                                                            
       2  
       3 +use std::collections::BTreeMap;                                
       4 +use std::path::Path;                                           
       5 +                                                               
       6 +use anyhow::Result;                                            
       7 +use serde::Deserialize;                                        
       8 +                                                               
       9 +use super::read_jsonl;                                         
      10 +use crate::models::{Document, MetaValue};                      
      11 +                                                               
      12 +#[derive(Deserialize)]                                         
      13 +struct Raw {                                                   
      14 +    #[serde(default)]                                          
      15 +    content: String,                                           
      16 +    #[serde(default)]                                          
      17 +    file_id: String,                                           
      18 +    #[serde(default = "default_name")]                         
      19 +    file_name: String,                                         
      20 +    #[serde(default)]                                          
      21 +    file_type: String,                                         
      22 +    #[serde(default)]                                          
      23 +    extraction_method: String,                                 
      24 +    #[serde(default)]                                          
      25 +    channel_name: String,                                      
      26 +}                                                              
      27 +                                                               
      28 +fn default_name() -> String {                                  
      29 +    "unknown".into()                                           
      30 +}                                                              
      31 +                                                               
      32 +pub fn normalize(raw_dir: &Path) -> Result<Vec<Document>> {    
      33 +    let records = read_jsonl(&raw_dir.join("files_extracted.jso
         +nl"))?;                                                        
      34 +    let mut out = Vec::with_capacity(records.len());           
      35 +    for v in records {                                         
      36 +        let r: Raw = match serde_json::from_value(v) {         
      37 +            Ok(r) => r,                                        
      38 +            Err(_) => continue,                                
      39 +        };                                                     
      40 +        let content = r.content.trim().to_string();            
      41 +        if content.len() < 20 {                                
      42 +            continue;                                          
      43 +        }                                                      
      44 +        let mut metadata = BTreeMap::new();                    
      45 +        metadata.insert("file_type".into(), MetaValue::Str(r.fi
         +le_type));                                                     
      46 +        metadata.insert("extraction_method".into(), MetaValue::
         +Str(r.extraction_method));                                     
      47 +        metadata.insert("channel_name".into(), MetaValue::Str(r
         +.channel_name));                                               
      48 +        out.push(Document {                                    
      49 +            id: format!("file:{}", r.file_id),                 
      50 +            source: "file".into(),                             
      51 +            content,                                           
      52 +            title: r.file_name,                                
      53 +            metadata,                                          
      54 +        });                                                    
      55 +    }                                                          
      56 +    Ok(out)                                                    
      57 +}

       1 +//! Source code files вҶ’ Document.

       3 +use std::collections::BTreeMap;

         +guage));

         +ize_bytes as i64));

      60 +            if c.content.is_empty() {                          
      61 +                continue;                                      
      62 +            }                                                  
      63 +            let prefix = match c.path.as_deref() {             
      64 +                Some(p) if !p.is_empty() => format!("{} on {p}"
         +, c.author),                                                   
      65 +                _ => c.author.clone(),                         
      66 +            };                                                 
      67 +            parts.push(format!("{prefix}: {}", c.content));    
      68 +        }                                                      
      69 +                                                               
      70 +        let content = parts.join("\n");                        
      71 +        if content.len() < 20 {                                
      72 +            continue;                                          
      73 +        }                                                      
      74 +                                                               
      75 +        let title_full = format!("{} PR#{}: {}", r.repo, r.pr_i
         +d, r.title);                                                   
      76 +        let title: String = title_full.chars().take(120).collec
         +t();                                                           
      77 +                                                               
      78 +        let mut metadata = BTreeMap::new();                    
      79 +        metadata.insert("repo".into(), MetaValue::Str(r.repo.cl
         +one()));                                                       
      80 +        metadata.insert("state".into(), MetaValue::Str(r.state)
         +);                                                             
      81 +        metadata.insert("source_branch".into(), MetaValue::Str(
         +r.source_branch));                                             
      82 +        metadata.insert("target_branch".into(), MetaValue::Str(
         +r.target_branch));                                             
      83 +        metadata.insert("comment_count".into(), MetaValue::Int(
         +r.comments.len() as i64));                                     
      84 +        metadata.insert("approvals".into(), MetaValue::Str(r.ap
         +provals.join(", ")));                                          
      85 +                                                               
      86 +        out.push(Document {                                    
      87 +            id: format!("bitbucket:{}:{}", r.repo, r.pr_id),   
      88 +            source: "bitbucket".into(),                        
      89 +            content,                                           
      90 +            title,                                             
      91 +            metadata,                                          
      92 +        });                                                    
      93 +    }                                                          
      94 +    Ok(out)                                                    
      95 +}

        1 +//! Ingest orchestrator: scrape вҶ’ normalize вҶ’ chunk вҶ’ embed вҶ’ 
          +store.                                                        
        2 +//!                                                           
        3 +//! Mirrors `src/ragrep/ingest/pipeline.py::ingest`.          
        4  
        5 +use std::collections::BTreeMap;                               
        6 +use std::fs::File;                                            
        7 +use std::io::{BufWriter, Write};                              
        8 +use std::path::{Path, PathBuf};                               
        9 +use std::time::Instant;                                       
       10 +                                                              
       11 +use anyhow::{Context, Result};                                
       12 +                                                              
       13 +use crate::config::Config;                                    
       14 +use crate::embed;                                             
       15 +use crate::index::{bm25::Bm25, store};                        
       16 +use crate::ingest::{chunk, normalize};                        
       17 +use crate::models::IngestStats;                               
       18 +                                                              
       19 +const EMBEDDINGS_FILE: &str = "embeddings.bin";               
       20 +const CHECKPOINT_FILE: &str = ".embed_checkpoint.bin";        
       21 +                                                              
       22 +pub fn run(cfg: &Config, force: bool, source_filter: Option<&s
          +tr>) -> Result<IngestStats> {                                 
       23 +    let start = Instant::now();                               
       24 +    let raw_dir = cfg.raw_dir();                              
       25 +    let index_dir = cfg.index_dir();                          
       26 +    std::fs::create_dir_all(&index_dir)                       
       27 +        .with_context(|| format!("creating {}", index_dir.disp
          +lay()))?;                                                     
       28 +                                                              
       29 +    // 1. Resolve embedder via factory                        
       30 +    let embedder = embed::make(&cfg.embedding.provider, &cfg.e
          +mbedding.model_name)?;                                        
       31 +    tracing::info!(                                           
       32 +        target: "ragrep::ingest",                             
       33 +        "embedder ready: provider={} model={} dim={}",        
       34 +        embedder.provider(),                                  
       35 +        embedder.model(),                                     
       36 +        embedder.dim()                                        
       37 +    );                                                        
       38 +                                                              
       39 +    // 2. Load per-(provider, model) cache (empty if --force o
          +r file absent)                                                
       40 +    let mut cache = if force {                                
       41 +        embed::cache::Cache::empty(embedder.provider(), embedd
          +er.model(), embedder.dim())                                   
       42 +    } else {                                                  
       43 +        embed::cache::load(&index_dir, embedder.provider(), em
          +bedder.model(), embedder.dim())?                              
       44 +    };                                                        
       45 +    tracing::info!(                                           
       46 +        target: "ragrep::ingest",                             
       47 +        "embed cache: {} entries",                            
       48 +        cache.len()                                           
       49 +    );                                                        
       50 +                                                              
       51 +    // 3. Normalize                                           
       52 +    tracing::info!(target: "ragrep::ingest", "step 1/4 normali
          +ze: reading {}", raw_dir.display());                          
       53 +    let mut docs = normalize::normalize_all(&raw_dir)?;       
       54 +    if let Some(s) = source_filter {                          
       55 +        docs.retain(|d| d.source == s);                       
       56 +        tracing::info!(target: "ragrep::ingest", "filtered to 
          +{} documents (source={s})", docs.len());                      
       57 +    }                                                         
       58 +    if docs.is_empty() {                                      
       59 +        tracing::warn!(target: "ragrep::ingest", "no documents
          + to ingest");                                                 
       60 +        return Ok(IngestStats::default());                    
       61 +    }                                                         
       62 +                                                              
       63 +    // 4. Chunk                                               
       64 +    tracing::info!(target: "ragrep::ingest", "step 2/4 chunk: 
          +{} docs", docs.len());                                        
       65 +    let chunks = chunk::all(&docs, cfg.ingest.max_chunk_tokens
          +, cfg.ingest.chunk_overlap_tokens);                           
       66 +                                                              
       67 +    // 5. Hash + diff vs cache                                
       68 +    tracing::info!(target: "ragrep::ingest", "step 3/4 embed: 
          +{} chunks", chunks.len());                                    
       69 +    let hashes: Vec<embed::cache::Hash> = chunks.iter().map(|c
          +| embed::cache::hash(&c.content)).collect();                  
       70 +    let to_embed_idx: Vec<usize> = hashes                     
       71 +        .iter()                                               
       72 +        .enumerate()                                          
       73 +        .filter_map(|(i, h)| if cache.contains(h) { None } els
          +e { Some(i) })                                                
       74 +        .collect();                                           
       75 +    let cached_count = chunks.len() - to_embed_idx.len();     
       76 +    tracing::info!(                                           
       77 +        target: "ragrep::ingest",                             
       78 +        "embed plan: {} new, {} cached",                      
       79 +        to_embed_idx.len(),                                   
       80 +        cached_count                                          
       81 +    );                                                        
       82 +                                                              
       83 +    // 6. Embed misses                                        
       84 +    if !to_embed_idx.is_empty() {                             
       85 +        let texts: Vec<&str> = to_embed_idx.iter().map(|i| chu
          +nks[*i].content.as_str()).collect();                          
       86 +        let checkpoint = index_dir.join(CHECKPOINT_FILE);     
       87 +        let new_embeddings = embedder                         
       88 +            .embed_documents(&texts, cfg.ingest.batch_size, So
          +me(&checkpoint))                                              
       89 +            .context("embedding new chunks")?;                
       90 +        for (j, idx) in to_embed_idx.iter().enumerate() {     
       91 +            cache.insert(hashes[*idx], new_embeddings[j].clone
          +());                                                          
       92 +        }                                                     
       93 +    }                                                         
       94 +                                                              
       95 +    // 7. Assemble full embedding matrix in chunk order       
       96 +    let mut embeddings: Vec<Vec<f32>> = Vec::with_capacity(chu
          +nks.len());                                                   
       97 +    for h in &hashes {                                        
       98 +        embeddings.push(                                      
       99 +            cache                                             
      100 +                .get(h)                                       
      101 +                .cloned()                                     
      102 +                .ok_or_else(|| anyhow::anyhow!("embedding miss
          +ing for hash after embed step"))?,                            
      103 +        );                                                    
      104 +    }                                                         
      105 +                                                              
      106 +    // 8. Save chunks + BM25 + embeddings (atomic) + cache    
      107 +    tracing::info!(target: "ragrep::ingest", "step 4/4 store: 
          +writing index files");                                        
      108 +    store::save_chunks(&index_dir, &chunks)?;                 
      109 +    let bm25 = Bm25::build(chunks.iter().map(|c| c.content.as_
          +str()));                                                      
      110 +    store::save_bm25(&index_dir, &bm25)?;                     
      111 +    save_embeddings(&index_dir, &embeddings, embedder.dim())?;
      112 +    embed::cache::save(&cache, &index_dir)?;                  
      113 +                                                              
      114 +    let elapsed = start.elapsed().as_secs_f64();              
      115 +                                                              
      116 +    let mut sources: BTreeMap<String, usize> = BTreeMap::new()
          +;                                                             
      117 +    for d in &docs {                                          
      118 +        *sources.entry(d.source.clone()).or_insert(0) += 1;   
      119 +    }                                                         
      120 +                                                              
      121 +    let stats = IngestStats {                                 
      122 +        documents: docs.len(),                                
      123 +        chunks: chunks.len(),                                 
      124 +        sources,                                              
      125 +        elapsed_s: elapsed,                                   
      126 +    };                                                        
      127 +                                                              
      128 +    tracing::info!(                                           
      129 +        target: "ragrep::ingest",                             
      130 +        "done: {} docs вҶ’ {} chunks ({} new, {} cached) in {:.1
          +}s",                                                          
      131 +        stats.documents,                                      
      132 +        stats.chunks,                                         
      133 +        to_embed_idx.len(),                                   
      134 +        cached_count,                                         
      135 +        stats.elapsed_s                                       
      136 +    );                                                        
      137 +    Ok(stats)                                                 
      138 +}                                                             
      139 +                                                              
      140 +fn embeddings_path(index_dir: &Path) -> PathBuf {             
      141 +    index_dir.join(EMBEDDINGS_FILE)                           
      142 +}                                                             
      143 +                                                              
      144 +fn save_embeddings(index_dir: &Path, embeddings: &[Vec<f32>], 
          +dim: usize) -> Result<()> {                                   
      145 +    let final_path = embeddings_path(index_dir);              
      146 +    let tmp = final_path.with_extension("bin.tmp");           
      147 +    let file = File::create(&tmp).with_context(|| format!("cre
          +ating {}", tmp.display()))?;                                  
      148 +    let mut w = BufWriter::new(file);                         
      149 +    for v in embeddings {                                     
      150 +        if v.len() != dim {                                   
      151 +            anyhow::bail!("embedding dim mismatch: expected {d
          +im}, got {}", v.len());                                       
      152 +        }                                                     
      153 +        w.write_all(bytemuck::cast_slice(v))?;                
      154 +    }                                                         
      155 +    w.flush()?;                                               
      156 +    drop(w);                                                  
      157 +    std::fs::rename(&tmp, &final_path)                        
      158 +        .with_context(|| format!("renaming {} вҶ’ {}", tmp.displ
          +ay(), final_path.display()))?;                                
      159 +    Ok(())                                                    
      160 +}

  вҺҝ В Added 190 lines
        1 +//! OpenAI embeddings вҖ” direct HTTP, no SDK.                  
        2 +//!                                                           
        3 +//! Mirrors `OpenAIEmbedder` from `src/ragrep/ingest/embed.py:
          +393`.                                                         
        4  
        5 +use std::env;                                                 
        6 +use std::path::Path;                                          
        7 +use std::thread;                                              
        8 +use std::time::Duration;                                      
        9 +                                                              
       10 +use anyhow::{anyhow, bail, Context, Result};                  
       11 +use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};                          
       12 +                                                              
       13 +use super::throttle::Throttle;                                
       14 +                                                              
       15 +const BASE: &str = "https://api.openai.com/v1";               
       16 +const ENV_KEY: &str = "OPENAI_API_KEY";                       
       17 +const REQUEST_TIMEOUT: Duration = Duration::from_secs(30);    
       18 +const PROVIDER: &str = "openai";                              
       19 +/// OpenAI's `/v1/embeddings` accepts up to 2048 inputs. We ca
          +p at 64 to mirror                                             
       20 +/// the Python implementation; smaller batches mean lower requ
          +est bursts under                                              
       21 +/// the same total throughput.                                
       22 +const MAX_API_BATCH: usize = 64;                              
       23 +const MAX_ATTEMPTS: u32 = 5;                                  
       24 +                                                              
       25 +/// Native dim per OpenAI model. `text-embedding-3-large` defa
          +ults to 3072                                                  
       26 +/// but supports the `dimensions` request param to truncate (w
          +e don't use                                                   
       27 +/// that; we pass the native dim through to the index).       
       28 +fn dim_for(model: &str) -> usize {                            
       29 +    match model {                                             
       30 +        "text-embedding-3-small" => 1536,                     
       31 +        "text-embedding-3-large" => 3072,                     
       32 +        "text-embedding-ada-002" => 1536,                     
       33 +        _ => 1536,                                            
       34 +    }                                                         
       35 +}                                                             
       36 +                                                              
       37 +pub struct Embedder {                                         
       38 +    api_key: String,                                          
       39 +    model: String,                                            
       40 +    dim: usize,                                               
       41 +}                                                             
       42 +                                                              
       43 +impl Embedder {                                               
       44 +    pub fn new(model: &str) -> Result<Self> {                 
       45 +        let api_key = env::var(ENV_KEY)                       
       46 +            .map_err(|_| anyhow!("{ENV_KEY} is not set (add to
          + .env or export it)"))?;                                      
       47 +        Ok(Self {                                             
       48 +            api_key,                                          
       49 +            model: model.to_string(),                         
       50 +            dim: dim_for(model),                              
       51 +        })                                                    
       52 +    }                                                         
       53 +}                                                             
       54 +                                                              
       55 +impl super::Embedder for Embedder {                           
       56 +    fn provider(&self) -> &str {                              
       57 +        PROVIDER                                              
       58 +    }                                                         
       59 +    fn model(&self) -> &str {                                 
       60 +        &self.model                                           
       61 +    }                                                         
       62 +    fn dim(&self) -> usize {                                  
       63 +        self.dim                                              
       64 +    }                                                         
       65 +                                                              
       66 +    fn embed_query(&self, text: &str) -> Result<Vec<f32>> {   
       67 +        let mut out = embed_call(&self.api_key, &self.model, &
          +[text])?;                                                     
       68 +        Ok(normalize(out.swap_remove(0)))                     
       69 +    }                                                         
       70 +                                                              
       71 +    fn embed_documents(                                       
       72 +        &self,                                                
       73 +        texts: &[&str],                                       
       74 +        batch_size: usize,                                    
       75 +        _checkpoint: Option<&Path>,                           
       76 +    ) -> Result<Vec<Vec<f32>>> {                              
       77 +        let total = texts.len();                              
       78 +        let api_batch = batch_size.clamp(1, MAX_API_BATCH);   
       79 +                                                              
       80 +        let mut all: Vec<Vec<f32>> = Vec::with_capacity(total)
          +;                                                             
       81 +        // OpenAI's normal tier has generous rate limits; star
          +t fast.                                                       
       82 +        let mut throttle = Throttle::new(0.5, 0.05, 30.0);    
       83 +        let mut i = 0usize;                                   
       84 +                                                              
       85 +        while i < total {                                     
       86 +            let end = (i + api_batch).min(total);             
       87 +            let batch: Vec<&str> = texts[i..end].to_vec();    
       88 +                                                              
       89 +            if i > 0 {                                        
       90 +                throttle.wait();                              
       91 +            }                                                 
       92 +                                                              
       93 +            let mut attempt = 0u32;                           
       94 +            loop {                                            
       95 +                attempt += 1;                                 
       96 +                match embed_call(&self.api_key, &self.model, &
          +batch) {                                                      
       97 +                    Ok(vs) => {                               
       98 +                        all.extend(vs.into_iter().map(normaliz
          +e));                                                          
       99 +                        throttle.on_success();                
      100 +                        break;                                
      101 +                    }                                         
      102 +                    Err(e) => {                               
      103 +                        let msg = format!("{e}");             
      104 +                        if msg.contains("HTTP 429") || msg.con
          +tains("HTTP 503") {                                           
      105 +                            if attempt >= MAX_ATTEMPTS {      
      106 +                                return Err(e).context(format!(
      107 +                                    "OpenAI embed: rate-limit 
          +exhausted at {}/{}",                                          
      108 +                                    all.len(),                
      109 +                                    total                     
      110 +                                ));                           
      111 +                            }                                 
      112 +                            throttle.on_rate_limit(None);     
      113 +                            tracing::warn!(                   
      114 +                                target: "ragrep::embed",      
      115 +                                "openai rate-limited; sleeping
          + {:.1}s (attempt {}/{})",                                     
      116 +                                throttle.delay,               
      117 +                                attempt,                      
      118 +                                MAX_ATTEMPTS                  
      119 +                            );                                
      120 +                            thread::sleep(Duration::from_secs_
          +f32(throttle.delay));                                         
      121 +                            continue;                         
      122 +                        }                                     
      123 +                        return Err(e).context(format!(        
      124 +                            "OpenAI embed failed at {}/{}",   
      125 +                            all.len(),                        
      126 +                            total                             
      127 +                        ));                                   
      128 +                    }                                         
      129 +                }                                             
      130 +            }                                                 
      131 +                                                              
      132 +            i = end;                                          
      133 +        }                                                     
      134 +                                                              
      135 +        Ok(all)                                               
      136 +    }                                                         
      137 +}                                                             
      138 +                                                              
      139 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                          
      140 +struct EmbedRequest<'a> {                                     
      141 +    model: &'a str,                                           
      142 +    input: &'a [&'a str],                                     
      143 +}                                                             
      144 +                                                              
      145 +#[derive(Deserialize)]                                        
      146 +struct EmbedResponse {                                        
      147 +    data: Vec<EmbedItem>,                                     
      148 +}                                                             
      149 +                                                              
      150 +#[derive(Deserialize)]                                        
      151 +struct EmbedItem {                                            
      152 +    embedding: Vec<f32>,                                      
      153 +    index: usize,                                             
      154 +}                                                             
      155 +                                                              
      156 +fn embed_call(api_key: &str, model: &str, inputs: &[&str]) -> 
          +Result<Vec<Vec<f32>>> {                                       
      157 +    let client = reqwest::blocking::Client::builder()         
      158 +        .timeout(REQUEST_TIMEOUT)                             
      159 +        .build()                                              
      160 +        .context("building HTTP client")?;                    
      161 +    let resp = client                                         
      162 +        .post(format!("{BASE}/embeddings"))                   
      163 +        .bearer_auth(api_key)                                 
      164 +        .json(&EmbedRequest { model, input: inputs })         
      165 +        .send()                                               
      166 +        .context("sending embed request")?;                   
      167 +                                                              
      168 +    if !resp.status().is_success() {                          
      169 +        let status = resp.status();                           
      170 +        let body = resp.text().unwrap_or_default();           
      171 +        bail!("OpenAI embed failed: HTTP {status} вҖ” {body}"); 
      172 +    }                                                         
      173 +    let mut payload: EmbedResponse = resp.json().context("pars
          +ing embed response")?;                                        
      174 +    if payload.data.is_empty() {                              
      175 +        bail!("OpenAI embed: empty data array");              
      176 +    }                                                         
      177 +    payload.data.sort_by_key(|x| x.index);                    
      178 +    Ok(payload.data.into_iter().map(|x| x.embedding).collect()
          +)                                                             
      179 +}                                                             
      180 +                                                              
      181 +/// L2-normalize. OpenAI returns un-normalized vectors; the re
          +st of the                                                     
      182 +/// pipeline assumes вҖ–vвҖ– = 1 (cosine via inner product on a fl
          +at IP index).                                                 
      183 +fn normalize(mut v: Vec<f32>) -> Vec<f32> {                   
      184 +    let norm = v.iter().map(|x| x * x).sum::<f32>().sqrt();   
      185 +    if norm > 0.0 {                                           
      186 +        for x in &mut v {                                     
      187 +            *x /= norm;                                       
      188 +        }                                                     
      189 +    }                                                         
      190 +    v                                                         
      191 +}

        1 +//! Google Gemini embeddings вҖ” direct HTTP, no SDK.           
        2 +//!                                                           
        3 +//! Mirrors `GeminiEmbedder` from `src/ragrep/ingest/embed.py:
          +564`. Uses the                                                
        4 +//! `batchEmbedContents` endpoint for the document path (up to
          + 100 inputs                                                   
        5 +//! per call) and `embedContent` for one-shot queries.

        8 +use std::path::Path;                                          
        9 +use std::thread;                                              
       10 +use std::time::Duration;                                      
       11 +                                                              
       12 +use anyhow::{anyhow, bail, Context, Result};                  
       13 +use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};                          
       14 +                                                              
       15 +use super::throttle::Throttle;                                
       16 +

          +v1beta";                                                      
       18 +const ENV_KEY: &str = "GEMINI_API_KEY";

       20 +const PROVIDER: &str = "gemini";

       26 +                                                              
       27 +fn dim_for(model: &str) -> usize {

       29 +        "gemini-embedding-001" | "text-embedding-004" => 3072,
       30 +        _ => 3072,                                            
       31 +    }                                                         
       32 +}                                                             
       33 +                                                              
       34 +pub struct Embedder {                                         
       35 +    api_key: String,

       50 +}                                                             
       51 +

       53 +    fn provider(&self) -> &str {                              
       54 +        PROVIDER                                              
       55 +    }                                                         
       56 +    fn model(&self) -> &str {

       61 +    }                                                         
       62 +                                                              
       63 +    fn embed_query(&self, text: &str) -> Result<Vec<f32>> {   
       64 +        let v = embed_one(&self.api_key, &self.model, text, TA
          +SK_QUERY)?;                                                   
       65 +        Ok(normalize(v))                                      
       66 +    }                                                         
       67 +                                                              
       68 +    fn embed_documents(                                       
       69 +        &self,                                                
       70 +        texts: &[&str],                                       
       71 +        batch_size: usize,                                    
       72 +        _checkpoint: Option<&Path>,                           
       73 +    ) -> Result<Vec<Vec<f32>>> {                              
       74 +        let total = texts.len();                              
       75 +        let api_batch = batch_size.clamp(1, MAX_API_BATCH);   
       76 +                                                              
       77 +        let mut all: Vec<Vec<f32>> = Vec::with_capacity(total)
          +;                                                             
       78 +        // Gemini's free tier has tighter limits than OpenAI; 
          +start moderate.                                               
       79 +        let mut throttle = Throttle::new(2.0, 0.1, 60.0);     
       80 +        let mut i = 0usize;                                   
       81 +                                                              
       82 +        while i < total {                                     
       83 +            let end = (i + api_batch).min(total);             
       84 +            let batch: Vec<&str> = texts[i..end].to_vec();    
       85 +                                                              
       86 +            if i > 0 {                                        
       87 +                throttle.wait();                              
       88 +            }                                                 
       89 +

       91 +            loop {                                            
       92 +                attempt += 1;                                 
       93 +                match embed_batch(&self.api_key, &self.model, 
          +&batch) {                                                     
       94 +                    Ok(vs) => {                               
       95 +                        all.extend(vs.into_iter().map(normaliz
          +e));                                                          
       96 +                        throttle.on_success();                
       97 +                        break;                                
       98 +                    }                                         
       99 +                    Err(e) => {                               
      100 +                        let msg = format!("{e}");             
      101 +                        if msg.contains("HTTP 429") || msg.con
          +tains("RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED") {                                 
      102 +                            if attempt >= MAX_ATTEMPTS {      
      103 +                                return Err(e).context(format!(
      104 +                                    "Gemini embed: rate-limit 
          +exhausted at {}/{}",                                          
      105 +                                    all.len(),                
      106 +                                    total                     
      107 +                                ));
