      112 +                                "gemini rate-limited; sleeping
          + {:.1}s (attempt {}/{})",                                     
      113 +                                throttle.delay,               
      114 +                                attempt,                      
      115 +                                MAX_ATTEMPTS                  
      116 +                            );

          +f32(throttle.delay));

      120 +                        return Err(e).context(format!(

      123 +                            total                             
      124 +                        ));                                   
      125 +                    }                                         
      126 +                }

      129 +            i = end;                                          
      130 +        }                                                     
      131 +                                                              
      132 +        Ok(all)                                               
      133 +    }                                                         
      134 +}                                                             
      135 +                                                              
      136 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                          
      137 +struct Content<'a> {                                          
      138 +    parts: Vec<Part<'a>>,                                     
      139 +}                                                             
      140 +                                                              
      141 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                          
      142 +struct Part<'a> {                                             
      143 +    text: &'a str,                                            
      144 +}                                                             
      145 +                                                              
      146 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                          
      147 +struct EmbedOneRequest<'a> {                                  
      148 +    model: String,                                            
      149 +    content: Content<'a>,                                     
      150 +    #[serde(rename = "taskType")]                             
      151 +    task_type: &'a str,                                       
      152 +}                                                             
      153 +                                                              
      154 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                          
      155 +struct BatchRequest<'a> {                                     
      156 +    requests: Vec<EmbedOneRequest<'a>>,                       
      157 +}                                                             
      158 +                                                              
      159 +#[derive(Deserialize)]                                        
      160 +struct EmbeddingValues {                                      
      161 +    values: Vec<f32>,                                         
      162 +}                                                             
      163 +                                                              
      164 +#[derive(Deserialize)]                                        
      165 +struct OneResponse {                                          
      166 +    embedding: EmbeddingValues,                               
      167 +}                                                             
      168 +                                                              
      169 +#[derive(Deserialize)]                                        
      170 +struct BatchResponse {                                        
      171 +    embeddings: Vec<EmbeddingValues>,                         
      172 +}                                                             
      173 +                                                              
      174 +fn embed_one(api_key: &str, model: &str, text: &str, task_type
          +: &str) -> Result<Vec<f32>> {                                 
      175 +    let url = format!("{BASE}/models/{model}:embedContent?key=
          +{api_key}");                                                  
      176 +    let body = EmbedOneRequest {                              
      177 +        model: format!("models/{model}"),                     
      178 +        content: Content { parts: vec![Part { text }] },      
      179 +        task_type,                                            
      180 +    };                                                        
      181 +    let client = reqwest::blocking::Client::builder()         
      182 +        .timeout(REQUEST_TIMEOUT)                             
      183 +        .build()                                              
      184 +        .context("building HTTP client")?;                    
      185 +    let resp = client                                         
      186 +        .post(&url)                                           
      187 +        .json(&body)                                          
      188 +        .send()                                               
      189 +        .context("sending Gemini embed request")?;            
      190 +    if !resp.status().is_success() {                          
      191 +        let status = resp.status();                           
      192 +        let txt = resp.text().unwrap_or_default();            
      193 +        bail!("Gemini embed failed: HTTP {status} вҖ” {txt}");  
      194 +    }                                                         
      195 +    let payload: OneResponse = resp.json().context("parsing Ge
          +mini embed response")?;                                       
      196 +    Ok(payload.embedding.values)                              
      197 +}                                                             
      198 +                                                              
      199 +fn embed_batch(api_key: &str, model: &str, texts: &[&str]) -> 
          +Result<Vec<Vec<f32>>> {                                       
      200 +    let url = format!("{BASE}/models/{model}:batchEmbedContent
          +s?key={api_key}");                                            
      201 +    let model_path = format!("models/{model}");               
      202 +    let requests: Vec<EmbedOneRequest> = texts                
      203 +        .iter()                                               
      204 +        .map(|t| EmbedOneRequest {                            
      205 +            model: model_path.clone(),                        
      206 +            content: Content { parts: vec![Part { text: t }] }
          +,                                                             
      207 +            task_type: TASK_DOCUMENT,                         
      208 +        })                                                    
      209 +        .collect();                                           
      210 +    let body = BatchRequest { requests };                     
      211 +                                                              
      212 +    let client = reqwest::blocking::Client::builder()         
      213 +        .timeout(REQUEST_TIMEOUT)                             
      214 +        .build()                                              
      215 +        .context("building HTTP client")?;                    
      216 +    let resp = client                                         
      217 +        .post(&url)                                           
      218 +        .json(&body)                                          
      219 +        .send()                                               
      220 +        .context("sending Gemini batch embed request")?;      
      221 +    if !resp.status().is_success() {                          
      222 +        let status = resp.status();                           
      223 +        let txt = resp.text().unwrap_or_default();            
      224 +        bail!("Gemini batch embed failed: HTTP {status} вҖ” {txt
          +}");                                                          
      225 +    }                                                         
      226 +    let payload: BatchResponse = resp.json().context("parsing 
          +Gemini batch response")?;                                     
      227 +    Ok(payload.embeddings.into_iter().map(|e| e.values).collec
          +t())                                                          
      228 +}                                                             
      229 +                                                              
      230 +fn normalize(mut v: Vec<f32>) -> Vec<f32> {                   
      231 +    let norm = v.iter().map(|x| x * x).sum::<f32>().sqrt();   
      232 +    if norm > 0.0 {                                           
      233 +        for x in &mut v {                                     
      234 +            *x /= norm;                                       
      235 +        }                                                     
      236 +    }                                                         
      237 +    v                                                         
      238 +}

вҸә Write(rust/src/serve/search.rs)
  вҺҝ В Added 240 lines
        1 +//! `GET /search` handler. JSON response shape matches `src/ra
          +grep/server.py::search`.                                      
        2  
        3 +use std::sync::Arc;                                           
        4 +                                                              
        5 +use anyhow::{anyhow, bail, Result};                           
        6 +use axum::{                                                   
        7 +    extract::{Query, State},                                  
        8 +    http::StatusCode,                                         
        9 +    Json,                                                     
       10 +};                                                            
       11 +use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};                          
       12 +use serde_json::json;                                         
       13 +                                                              
       14 +use super::AppState;                                          
       15 +use crate::models::{MetaValue, SearchResult};                 
       16 +use crate::query;                                             
       17 +use crate::query::filters;                                    
       18 +                                                              
       19 +#[derive(Deserialize, Clone)]                                 
       20 +pub struct SearchQuery {                                      
       21 +    pub q: String,                                            
       22 +    #[serde(default = "default_mode")]                        
       23 +    pub mode: String,                                         
       24 +    #[serde(default = "default_n")]                           
       25 +    pub n: usize,                                             
       26 +    pub source: Option<String>,                               
       27 +    pub filter: Option<String>,                               
       28 +    pub after: Option<String>,                                
       29 +    pub before: Option<String>,                               
       30 +    #[serde(default = "default_context")]                     
       31 +    pub context: usize,                                       
       32 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
       33 +    pub full: bool,                                           
       34 +    #[serde(default = "default_true")]                        
       35 +    pub scores: bool,                                         
       36 +    #[serde(default)]                                         
       37 +    pub metadata: bool,                                       
       38 +}                                                             
       39 +                                                              
       40 +fn default_mode() -> String {                                 
       41 +    "grep".into()                                             
       42 +}                                                             
       43 +fn default_n() -> usize {                                     
       44 +    5                                                         
       45 +}                                                             
       46 +fn default_context() -> usize {                               
       47 +    300                                                       
       48 +}                                                             
       49 +fn default_true() -> bool {                                   
       50 +    true                                                      
       51 +}                                                             
       52 +                                                              
       53 +pub async fn handle(                                          
       54 +    State(state): State<Arc<AppState>>,                       
       55 +    Query(q): Query<SearchQuery>,                             
       56 +) -> Result<Json<serde_json::Value>, (StatusCode, Json<serde_j
          +son::Value>)> {                                               
       57 +    let state2 = Arc::clone(&state);                          
       58 +    let q2 = q.clone();                                       
       59 +    let result = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || do_search
          +(&state2, q2))                                                
       60 +        .await                                                
       61 +        .map_err(|e| internal(format!("join: {e}")))?;        
       62 +    match result {                                            
       63 +        Ok(payload) => Ok(Json(payload)),                     
       64 +        Err(e) => Err(client_or_internal(e)),                 
       65 +    }                                                         
       66 +}                                                             
       67 +                                                              
       68 +fn do_search(state: &AppState, q: SearchQuery) -> Result<serde
          +_json::Value> {                                               
       69 +    let filt_metadata = match &q.filter {                     
       70 +        Some(s) if !s.is_empty() => {                         
       71 +            let parts: Vec<String> = s.split(',').map(str::to_
          +string).collect();                                            
       72 +            filters::parse_filters(&parts)?                   
       73 +        }                                                     
       74 +        _ => Default::default(),                              
       75 +    };                                                        
       76 +    let after = q.after.as_deref().map(filters::parse_date).tr
          +anspose()?;                                                   
       77 +    let before = q.before.as_deref().map(filters::parse_date).
          +transpose()?;                                                 
       78 +    let filt = query::Filters {                               
       79 +        source: q.source.as_deref(),                          
       80 +        metadata: filt_metadata,                              
       81 +        after: after.as_deref(),                              
       82 +        before: before.as_deref(),                            
       83 +    };                                                        
       84 +                                                              
       85 +    let cfg = &state.cfg;                                     
       86 +                                                              
       87 +    match q.mode.as_str() {                                   
       88 +        "grep" => {                                           
       89 +            let r = query::grep(&state.chunks, &q.q, &filt, q.
          +n);                                                           
       90 +            Ok(json!({                                        
       91 +                "query": r.query,                             
       92 +                "mode": "grep",                               
       93 +                "total_matches": r.total_matches,             
       94 +                "results": format_hits(&r.hits, &q),          
       95 +            }))                                               
       96 +        }                                                     
       97 +        "semantic" => {                                       
       98 +            let emb = state.embedder.embed_query(&q.q)?;      
       99 +            let r = query::semantic(&state.flat, &state.chunks
          +, &q.q, &emb, &filt, q.n);                                    
      100 +            Ok(json!({                                        
      101 +                "query": r.query,                             
      102 +                "mode": "semantic",                           
      103 +                "results": format_hits(&r.hits, &q),          
      104 +            }))                                               
      105 +        }                                                     
      106 +        "hybrid" => {                                         
      107 +            let emb = state.embedder.embed_query(&q.q)?;      
      108 +            let opts = query::HybridOpts {                    
      109 +                n: q.n,                                       
      110 +                top_k_dense: cfg.retrieval.top_k_dense,       
      111 +                top_k_bm25: cfg.retrieval.top_k_bm25,         
      112 +                rerank_pool: (q.n * 4).max(20),               
      113 +                rrf_k: cfg.retrieval.rrf_k,                   
      114 +                rerank_provider: &cfg.reranker.provider,      
      115 +                rerank_model: &cfg.reranker.model_name,       
      116 +                filters: filt,                                
      117 +            };                                                
      118 +            let r = query::hybrid(&state.flat, &state.bm25, &s
          +tate.chunks, &q.q, &emb, opts)?;                              
      119 +            Ok(json!({                                        
      120 +                "query": r.query,                             
      121 +                "mode": "hybrid",                             
      122 +                "results": format_hits(&r.hits, &q),          
      123 +            }))                                               
      124 +        }                                                     
      125 +        m => bail!("invalid mode: {m}"),                      
      126 +    }                                                         
      127 +}                                                             
      128 +                                                              
      129 +#[derive(Serialize)]                                          
      130 +struct OutHit<'a> {                                           
      131 +    rank: usize,                                              
      132 +    id: &'a str,                                              
      133 +    source: &'a str,                                          
      134 +    title: String,                                            
      135 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      136 +    snippet: Option<String>,                                  
      137 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      138 +    content: Option<&'a str>,                                 
      139 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      140 +    rerank: Option<f32>,                                      
      141 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      142 +    rrf: Option<f32>,                                         
      143 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      144 +    dense: Option<f32>,                                       
      145 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      146 +    bm25: Option<f32>,                                        
      147 +    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]         
      148 +    metadata: Option<&'a std::collections::BTreeMap<String, Me
          +taValue>>,                                                    
      149 +}                                                             
      150 +                                                              
      151 +fn format_hits(hits: &[query::Hit], q: &SearchQuery) -> Vec<se
          +rde_json::Value> {                                            
      152 +    hits.iter()                                               
      153 +        .map(|h| {                                            
      154 +            let r = &h.result;                                
      155 +            let title = truncate_title(&r.title);             
      156 +            let (snippet_v, content_v) = if q.full {          
      157 +                (None, Some(r.content.as_str()))              
      158 +            } else if q.context > 0 {                         
      159 +                (Some(snippet(&r.content, q.context, &q.q)), N
          +one)                                                          
      160 +            } else {                                          
      161 +                (None, None)                                  
      162 +            };                                                
      163 +            let out = OutHit {                                
      164 +                rank: h.rank,                                 
      165 +                id: r.chunk_id.as_str(),                      
      166 +                source: r.source.as_str(),                    
      167 +                title,                                        
      168 +                snippet: snippet_v,                           
      169 +                content: content_v,                           
      170 +                rerank: opt_score(r.rerank_score, q.scores),  
      171 +                rrf: opt_score(r.rrf_score, q.scores),        
      172 +                dense: opt_score(r.dense_score, q.scores),    
      173 +                bm25: opt_score(r.bm25_score, q.scores),      
      174 +                metadata: if q.metadata { Some(&r.metadata) } 
          +else { None },                                                
      175 +            };                                                
      176 +            serde_json::to_value(&out).unwrap_or_else(|_| json
          +!({}))                                                        
      177 +        })                                                    
      178 +        .collect()                                            
      179 +}                                                             
      180 +                                                              
      181 +fn truncate_title(title: &str) -> String {                    
      182 +    let chars: Vec<char> = title.chars().collect();           
      183 +    if chars.len() <= 80 {                                    
      184 +        title.to_string()                                     
      185 +    } else {                                                  
      186 +        let mut s: String = chars[..77].iter().collect();     
      187 +        s.push_str("...");                                    
      188 +        s                                                     
      189 +    }                                                         
      190 +}                                                             
      191 +                                                              
      192 +fn opt_score(v: f32, on: bool) -> Option<f32> {               
      193 +    if on && v != 0.0 {                                       
      194 +        Some((v * 1000.0).round() / 1000.0)                   
      195 +    } else {                                                  
      196 +        None                                                  
      197 +    }                                                         
      198 +}                                                             
      199 +                                                              
      200 +fn snippet(content: &str, length: usize, term: &str) -> String
          + {                                                            
      201 +    let flat: String = content.chars().map(|c| if c == '\n' { 
          +' ' } else { c }).collect();                                  
      202 +    let trimmed = flat.trim();                                
      203 +    if length == 0 || length >= trimmed.chars().count() {     
      204 +        return trimmed.to_string();                           
      205 +    }                                                         
      206 +    let lower = trimmed.to_lowercase();                       
      207 +    if let Some(pos) = lower.find(&term.to_lowercase()) {     
      208 +        let prefix_chars = trimmed[..pos].chars().count();    
      209 +        let half_back = length / 4;                           
      210 +        let start = prefix_chars.saturating_sub(half_back);   
      211 +        let chars: Vec<char> = trimmed.chars().collect();     
      212 +        let end = (start + length).min(chars.len());          
      213 +        let mut s: String = chars[start..end].iter().collect()
          +;                                                             
      214 +        if start > 0 {                                        
      215 +            s.insert_str(0, "...");                           
      216 +        }                                                     
      217 +        if end < chars.len() {                                
      218 +            s.push_str("...");                                
      219 +        }                                                     
      220 +        return s;                                             
      221 +    }                                                         
      222 +    let chars: Vec<char> = trimmed.chars().collect();         
      223 +    let mut s: String = chars[..length.min(chars.len())].iter(
          +).collect();                                                  
      224 +    if chars.len() > length {                                 
      225 +        s.push_str("...");                                    
      226 +    }                                                         
      227 +    s                                                         
      228 +}                                                             
      229 +                                                              
      230 +fn internal(msg: String) -> (StatusCode, Json<serde_json::Valu
          +e>) {                                                         
      231 +    (StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, Json(json!({ "error": 
          +msg })))                                                      
      232 +}                                                             
      233 +                                                              
      234 +fn client_or_internal(e: anyhow::Error) -> (StatusCode, Json<s
          +erde_json::Value>) {                                          
      235 +    let msg = format!("{e}");                                 
      236 +    if msg.starts_with("invalid mode") || msg.contains("invali
          +d filter") || msg.contains("invalid date") {                  
      237 +        (StatusCode::BAD_REQUEST, Json(json!({ "error": msg })
          +))                                                            
      238 +    } else {                                                  
      239 +        internal(msg)                                         
      240 +    }                                                         
      241 +}                                                             

вҸә Now wire cli::serve::run:

вҸә Write(rust/src/cli/serve.rs)
  вҺҝ В Added 54 lines, removed 3 lines
       1  use std::path::PathBuf;
       2 +use std::sync::Arc;                                            
       3  
       4  use anyhow::Result;
       5  use clap::Args;

  What now works without any Python:
  - ragrep <term> вҖ” search local index, all 3 modes, all filters
  - ragrep <term> --server URL вҖ” search remote ragrep
  - ragrep ingest [--force] [--source X] вҖ” build index from raw_dir
  - ragrep serve вҖ” host the index over HTTP
  - ragrep rebuild-bm25 вҖ” rebuild BM25 from chunks
  - ragrep вҖ” splash

  What still requires Python:
  - make scrape вҖ” scrape sources into raw_dir (Phase 3 ports this)
  - tools/migrate.py вҖ” one-time pickle вҶ’ binary cache conversion (will keep)

  One bug to fix when you have time: ragrep ingest --source X currently replaces
   chunks.msgpack (only emits the X-source chunks) instead of merging with the
  existing chunks. The Python pipeline has the same shape, but this is broken UX
   вҖ” should either (a) merge on top of existing chunks/embeddings, or (b)
  prevent destructive partial ingest. Quick fix: load existing chunks for
  non-filtered sources, merge with newly-normalized X-source chunks. ~1 hour.

  Want me to:
